              <img alt="Jean Luc Picard 2364.jpg" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean_Luc_Picard_2364.jpg" data-image-name="Jean Luc Picard 2364.jpg" height="326" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/a/a0/Jean_Luc_Picard_2364.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/292?cb=20140811123837&amp;path-prefix=en" width="292"/>
             </a>
             <figcaption>
              <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean_Luc_Picard_2364.jpg">
              </a>
              <p class="caption">
               <a href="/wiki/Captain" title="Captain">
                Captain
               </a>
               Jean-Luc Picard (
               <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
                2364
               </a>
               )
              </p>
             </figcaption>
            </figure>
            <a href="/wiki/Captain" title="Captain">
             Captain
            </a>
            Jean-Luc Picard (
            <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
             2364
            </a>
            )
           </td>
          </tr>
         </table>
         <div style="margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           For the alien who impersonated him, please see
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard_(impostor)" title="Jean-Luc Picard (impostor)">
            Jean-Luc Picard (impostor)
           </a>
           .
          </i>
         </div>
         <div style="margin: 0 0 0 1em;">
          "
          <i>
           I've never known anyone with more drive, determination or more courage than Jean-Luc Picard.
          </i>
          "
         </div>
         <div style="margin: 0 0 1em 2em;">
          
          <b>
           J.P. Hanson
          </b>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/2367" title="2367">
           2367
          </a>
          ("
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds,_Part_II_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (TNG 4x01)">
            The Best of Both Worlds, Part II
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </div>
         <p>
          <b>
           Jean-Luc Picard
          </b>
          was a celebrated
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet" title="Starfleet">
           Starfleet
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Officer" title="Officer">
           officer
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Archaeologist" title="Archaeologist">
           archaeologist
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Diplomat" title="Diplomat">
           diplomat
          </a>
          who served during the latter two thirds of the
          <a href="/wiki/24th_century" title="24th century">
           24th century
          </a>
          . The highlights of his career were centered around assignments as
          <a href="/wiki/Commanding_officer" title="Commanding officer">
           commanding officer
          </a>
          of the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">
           Federation
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Starship" title="Starship">
           starships
          </a>
          :
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Stargazer" title="USS Stargazer">
           USS
           <i>
            Stargazer
           </i>
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-D)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-D)">
           USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -D
          </a>
          , and the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-E)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-E)">
           USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -E
          </a>
          . In these roles, Picard not only witnessed the major turning points of recent galactic history, but played a key role in them also, from making
          <a href="/wiki/First_contact" title="First contact">
           first contact
          </a>
          as
          <a href="/wiki/Captain" title="Captain">
           captain
          </a>
          of the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">
           Federation
          </a>
          's
          <a href="/wiki/Flagship" title="Flagship">
           flagship
          </a>
          with no fewer than 27
          <a href="/wiki/Alien" title="Alien">
           alien
          </a>
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Species" title="Species">
           species
          </a>
          , including the
          <a href="/wiki/Ferengi" title="Ferengi">
           Ferengi
          </a>
          and the
          <a href="/wiki/Borg" title="Borg">
           Borg
          </a>
          . He also became the
          <a href="/wiki/Q" title="Q">
           chief contact point
          </a>
          with the
          <a href="/wiki/Q_Continuum" title="Q Continuum">
           Q Continuum
          </a>
          , and served as
          <a href="/wiki/Arbiter_of_Succession" title="Arbiter of Succession">
           Arbiter of Succession
          </a>
          , where he presided over the investiture of
          <a href="/wiki/Chancellor" title="Chancellor">
           Chancellor
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Gowron" title="Gowron">
           Gowron
          </a>
          . Picard would expose the
          <a href="/wiki/Romulan_Star_Empire" title="Romulan Star Empire">
           Romulan Star Empire
          </a>
          as backers of his
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Duras_sisters" title="Duras sisters">
           chief rivals
          </a>
          , later aiding a
          <a href="/wiki/Romulan_underground_movement" title="Romulan underground movement">
           Romulan underground movement
          </a>
          of dissidents to gain a toehold on the
          <a href="/wiki/Romulus" title="Romulus">
           Romulan homeworld
          </a>
          . He continued to serve as captain of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E, the sixth Federation starship to bear the name, until at least
          <a href="/wiki/2379" title="2379">
           2379
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Battle_(episode)" title="The Battle (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Battle (TNG 1x09)">
            The Battle
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Last_Outpost_(episode)" title="The Last Outpost (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Last Outpost (TNG 1x05)">
            The Last Outpost
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Q_Who_(episode)" title="Q Who (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Q Who (TNG 2x16)">
            Q Who
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Encounter_at_Farpoint_(episode)" title="Encounter at Farpoint (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Encounter at Farpoint (TNG 1x01/02)">
            Encounter at Farpoint
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/All_Good_Things..._(episode)" title="All Good Things... (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="All Good Things... (TNG 7x25/26)">
            All Good Things...
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_(episode)" title="Redemption (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption (TNG 4x26)">
            Redemption
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_II_(episode)" title="Redemption II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption II (TNG 5x01)">
            Redemption II
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Unification_II_(episode)" title="Unification II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Unification II (TNG 5x08)">
            Unification II
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">
           Biography
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit Biography section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Childhood">
           Childhood
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit Childhood section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/7/7e/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_age_12.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120518113130&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, age 12" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_age_12.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, age 12.jpg" data-src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/7/7e/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_age_12.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120518113130&amp;path-prefix=en" height="201" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, age 12" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_age_12.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, age 12.jpg" height="201" src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/7/7e/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_age_12.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120518113130&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean-Luc_Picard,_age_12.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard, reverted to the age of 12
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Jean-Luc Picard was born in
          <a href="/wiki/La_Barre" title="La Barre">
           La Barre
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">
           France
          </a>
          on
          <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">
           Earth
          </a>
          to
          <a href="/wiki/Maurice_Picard" title="Maurice Picard">
           Maurice
          </a>
          and
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yvette_Gessard" title="Yvette Gessard">
           Yvette Picard
          </a>
          on
          <a href="/wiki/July" title="July">
           July 13
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/2305" title="2305">
           2305
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Conundrum_(episode)" title="Conundrum (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Conundrum (TNG 5x14)">
            Conundrum
           </span>
          </a>
          ") He and his elder brother,
          <a href="/wiki/Robert_Picard" title="Robert Picard">
           Robert
          </a>
          , spent their childhood tending to their family vineyards with their father. Concerned about the preservation of their familial values, Maurice and his wife educated their sons in the ancient traditions, avoiding, in particular, any superfluous
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Technology" title="Technology">
           technologies
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ") As a young boy, Jean-Luc watched his grandfather "deteriorate from a powerful, intelligent figure to a frail wisp of a man, who could barely make his own way home." (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Night_Terrors_(episode)" title="Night Terrors (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Night Terrors (TNG 4x17)">
            Night Terrors
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          As a child, Jean-Luc took
          <a href="/wiki/Piano" title="Piano">
           piano
          </a>
          lessons but eventually gave it up because he dreaded performing in front of an audience. In his later life, he would regret doing so because his playing used to please his mother. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Lessons_(episode)" title="Lessons (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Lessons (TNG 6x19)">
            Lessons
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Perfect_Mate_(episode)" title="The Perfect Mate (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Perfect Mate (TNG 5x21)">
            The Perfect Mate
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Young Jean-Luc dreamed of adventure and exploration. He was fond of
          <a href="/wiki/Starship" title="Starship">
           starships
          </a>
          , of which he liked to
          <a href="/wiki/Promellian_battle_cruiser" title="Promellian battle cruiser">
           build models
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Booby_Trap_(episode)" title="Booby Trap (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Booby Trap (TNG 3x06)">
            Booby Trap
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Moreover, he was captivated by the
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Phoenix" title="Phoenix">
            Phoenix
           </a>
          </i>
          , the first
          <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">
           Human
          </a>
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Warp" title="Warp">
           warp
          </a>
          -capable
          <a href="/wiki/Starship" title="Starship">
           starship
          </a>
          , which he admired several times at the
          <a href="/wiki/Smithsonian_Institution" title="Smithsonian Institution">
           Smithsonian Institution
          </a>
          . (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Like his nephew
          <a href="/wiki/Ren%C3%A9_Picard" title="Ren Picard">
           Ren
          </a>
          , Jean-Luc wrote a ribbon-winning report on starships. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Although Maurice intended his sons to work at the vineyards, it was obvious that since very early Jean-Luc knew he wanted to join
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet" title="Starfleet">
           Starfleet
          </a>
          , something that his father would never condone, up until his death. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Bloodlines_(episode)" title="Bloodlines (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Bloodlines (TNG 7x22)">
            Bloodlines
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Jean-Luc would later remember that he devoted his childhood for that end, which was like skipping that age altogether. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Suddenly_Human_(episode)" title="Suddenly Human (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Suddenly Human (TNG 4x04)">
            Suddenly Human
           </span>
          </a>
          ") His brother would later note that Jean-Luc always sought higher standards, such as becoming president of his school and later a valedictorian and even an athletic champion. Robert was also jealous seeing Picard being the favored son and getting away after his mischiefs. Sometimes Robert had to bully his younger brother.  (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           Despite Picard having been born in
           <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">
            France
           </a>
           , he had a distinct
           <a href="/wiki/English" title="English">
            English
           </a>
           accent. According to
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Code_of_Honor_(episode)" title="Code of Honor (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Code of Honor (TNG 1x04)">
             Code of Honor
            </span>
           </a>
           ", by the
           <a href="/wiki/24th_century" title="24th century">
            24th century
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">
            French
           </a>
           was considered an archaic
           <a href="/wiki/Language" title="Language">
            language
           </a>
           . Picard remembered French children's songs like "
           <a href="/wiki/Fr%C3%A8re_Jacques" title="Frre Jacques">
            Frre Jacques
           </a>
           ," as mentioned in
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Disaster_(episode)" title="Disaster (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Disaster (TNG 5x05)">
             Disaster
            </span>
           </a>
           " and played by him on the Ressikan flute in
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/The_Inner_Light_(episode)" title="The Inner Light (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Inner Light (TNG 5x25)">
             The Inner Light
            </span>
           </a>
           ". He also occasionally cursed "merde" in times of stress, such as in "
           <a href="/wiki/The_Last_Outpost_(episode)" title="The Last Outpost (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Last Outpost (TNG 1x05)">
             The Last Outpost
            </span>
           </a>
           " and "
           <a href="/wiki/Elementary,_Dear_Data_(episode)" title="Elementary, Dear Data (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Elementary, Dear Data (TNG 2x03)">
             Elementary, Dear Data
            </span>
           </a>
           ", and spoke at least basic
           <a href="/wiki/French" title="French">
            French
           </a>
           ("
           <a href="/wiki/11001001_(episode)" title="11001001 (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="11001001 (TNG 1x15)">
             11001001
            </span>
           </a>
           ").
          </i>
         </div>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Academy_years">
           Academy years
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit Academy years section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/8/82/Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100823195916&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-LucPicardCadet" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/8/82/Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100823195916&amp;path-prefix=en" height="343" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Jean-LucPicardCadet" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg" height="343" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/8/82/Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100823195916&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean-LucPicardCadet.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Cadet Picard during his Academy years
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Jean-Luc caused "quite a stir" by leaving his family's generational vineyard and applying to
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet_Academy" title="Starfleet Academy">
           Starfleet Academy
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Although he failed to gain entry on his first attempt, Picard succeeded in his second attempt in
          <a href="/wiki/2323" title="2323">
           2323
          </a>
          . He subsequently became one of the most outstanding
          <a href="/wiki/Cadet" title="Cadet">
           cadets
          </a>
          in his class. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Coming_of_Age_(episode)" title="Coming of Age (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Coming of Age (TNG 1x19)">
            Coming of Age
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_First_Duty_(episode)" title="The First Duty (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The First Duty (TNG 5x19)">
            The First Duty
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard's career at the Academy was difficult, at best  years later, Picard credited Academy groundskeeper
          <a href="/wiki/Boothby" title="Boothby">
           Boothby
          </a>
          with helping him develop a mature attitude. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_First_Duty_(episode)" title="The First Duty (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The First Duty (TNG 5x19)">
            The First Duty
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Among Picard's friends at the Academy were
          <a href="/wiki/Donald_Varley" title="Donald Varley">
           Donald Varley
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Cortan_Zweller" title="Cortan Zweller">
           Cortan Zweller
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Marta_Batanides" title="Marta Batanides">
           Marta Batanides
          </a>
          , and an acquaintance called "
          <a href="/wiki/A.F." title="A.F.">
           A.F.
          </a>
          ", whom he blamed for his failed semester of
          <a href="/wiki/Organic_Chemistry" title="Organic Chemistry">
           Organic Chemistry
          </a>
          and whose initials Picard carved into Boothby's prized elm. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Contagion_(episode)" title="Contagion (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Contagion (TNG 2x11)">
            Contagion
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Game_(episode)" title="The Game (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Game (TNG 5x06)">
            The Game
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Peter_David" title="Peter David">
            Peter David
           </a>
           's
          </i>
          Star Trek
          <i>
           novels say another Academy classmate of Picard's was Morgan Korsmo, who was later killed fighting the
           <a href="/wiki/Borg" title="Borg">
            Borg
           </a>
           just before the start of the
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_New_Frontier" title="Star Trek: New Frontier">
           Star Trek: New Frontier
          </a>
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Novels" title="Novels">
            novels
           </a>
           . The
           <a href="/wiki/Starfleet_Corps_of_Engineers" title="Starfleet Corps of Engineers">
            Starfleet Corps of Engineers
           </a>
           <a href="/wiki/EBook" title="EBook">
            eBook
           </a>
           series says Captain David Gold was an upperclassman that freshman Picard beat in the Academy marathon.
          </i>
         </div>
         <p>
          At the Academy, Picard developed an interest in
          <a href="/wiki/Archaeology" title="Archaeology">
           archaeology
          </a>
          . His
          <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">
           professor
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Richard_Galen" title="Richard Galen">
           Richard Galen
          </a>
          , encouraged him to continue in this field, but Picard ultimately refused his offer of becoming an archaeologist. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Chase_(episode)" title="The Chase (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Chase (TNG 6x20)">
            The Chase
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard also excelled in sports. He won the
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet_Academy_marathon" title="Starfleet Academy marathon">
           Starfleet Academy marathon
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/April" title="April">
           April
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/2323" title="2323">
           2323
          </a>
          on
          <a href="/wiki/Danula_II" title="Danula II">
           Danula II
          </a>
          , becoming the first freshman to win the race. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds,_Part_II_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (TNG 4x01)">
            The Best of Both Worlds, Part II
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <a href="/wiki/Picard_family_album" title="Picard family album">
           Picard family album
          </a>
          ) During a
          <a href="/wiki/Wrestling" title="Wrestling">
           wrestling
          </a>
          match, Picard caught a
          <a href="/wiki/Ligonian" title="Ligonian">
           Ligonian
          </a>
          with a reverse body lift and pinned him down in the first fourteen seconds. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_First_Duty_(episode)" title="The First Duty (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The First Duty (TNG 5x19)">
            The First Duty
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          During his sophomore year, Picard was assigned to training on
          <a href="/wiki/Morikin_VII" title="Morikin VII">
           Morikin VII
          </a>
          where he had his first encounter with
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nausicaans" title="Nausicaans">
           Nausicaans
          </a>
          , who had an
          <a href="/wiki/Outpost" title="Outpost">
           outpost
          </a>
          on a nearby
          <a href="/wiki/Asteroid" title="Asteroid">
           asteroid
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          <br/>
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           The film
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            Star Trek Nemesis
           </span>
          </a>
          <i>
           seems to suggest that
           <a href="/wiki/Beverly_Crusher" title="Beverly Crusher">
            Beverly Crusher
           </a>
           knew and remembered Picard from his Academy days as being "cocky." This would be impossible, however, as Crusher was born a
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Year" title="Year">
            year
           </a>
           after Picard entered the Academy and would only be around three years old when he graduated. However, she might just have been referring to stories she heard about him from these days.
          </i>
          Nemesis
          <i>
           also depicts a younger Picard as being completely bald while at the Academy, though both "
           <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
             Tapestry
            </span>
           </a>
           " and "
           <a href="/wiki/Violations_(episode)" title="Violations (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Violations (TNG 5x12)">
             Violations
            </span>
           </a>
           " show him as having a full head of hair after this period, though it is entirely possible that he chose to shave his head in his youth. Indeed Picard's clone, Shinzon, who was of a similar age to Picard in his Academy years, shows the clear shadow of hair growth which would seemingly support the idea that Picard shaved his head at one point during his Academy years.
          </i>
         </div>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Starfleet_career">
           Early Starfleet career
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit Early Starfleet career section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/96/Jean-Luc_Picard_stabbed.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20050918033137&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard stabbed" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard_stabbed.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard stabbed.jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/96/Jean-Luc_Picard_stabbed.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20050918033137&amp;path-prefix=en" height="152" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard stabbed" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard_stabbed.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard stabbed.jpg" height="152" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/96/Jean-Luc_Picard_stabbed.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20050918033137&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean-Luc_Picard_stabbed.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Ensign Picard stabbed
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Shortly upon graduation in
          <a href="/wiki/2327" title="2327">
           2327
          </a>
          , Picard's promising career nearly ended abruptly during a layover at
          <a href="/wiki/Starbase_Earhart" title="Starbase Earhart">
           Starbase Earhart
          </a>
          . During a bar brawl over a rigged game of
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Dom-jot" title="Dom-jot">
            dom-jot
           </a>
          </i>
          , he was stabbed through the
          <a href="/wiki/Heart" title="Heart">
           heart
          </a>
          by a
          <a href="/wiki/Nausicaan" title="Nausicaan">
           Nausicaan
          </a>
          , and had to undergo emergency surgery to
          <a href="/wiki/Artificial_heart" title="Artificial heart">
           replace his heart
          </a>
          . He later related to
          <a href="/wiki/Wesley_Crusher" title="Wesley Crusher">
           Wesley Crusher
          </a>
          that he laughed after looking down to see the knife protruding from his chest. This event helped him realize how fragile life could be, and thus made him more willing to take risks and make his mark in the universe, which he only realized when Q proposed him to change this event in
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Samaritan_Snare_(episode)" title="Samaritan Snare (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Samaritan Snare (TNG 2x17)">
            Samaritan Snare
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          As an
          <a href="/wiki/Ensign" title="Ensign">
           ensign
          </a>
          , Picard was posted to the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Reliant_(24th_century)" title="USS Reliant (24th century)">
           USS
           <i>
            Reliant
           </i>
          </a>
          , where he served with
          <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant" title="Lieutenant">
           Lieutenant
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Nakamura" title="Nakamura">
           Nakamura
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Measure_Of_A_Man_(episode)" title="The Measure Of A Man (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Measure Of A Man (TNG 2x09)">
            The Measure Of A Man
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          As a
          <a href="/wiki/Junior_officer" title="Junior officer">
           junior officer
          </a>
          , Picard was the closest of friends with
          <a href="/wiki/Walker_Keel" title="Walker Keel">
           Walker Keel
          </a>
          , and also became friends with
          <a href="/wiki/Jack_Crusher" title="Jack Crusher">
           Jack Crusher
          </a>
          and his
          <a href="/wiki/Fianc%C3%A9e" title="Fiance">
           fiance
          </a>
          ,
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Beverly_Howard" title="Beverly Howard">
           Beverly Howard
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Conspiracy_(episode)" title="Conspiracy (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Conspiracy (TNG 1x25)">
            Conspiracy
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Journey%27s_End_(episode)" title="Journey's End (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Journey's End (TNG 7x20)">
            Journey's End
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Attached_(episode)" title="Attached (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Attached (TNG 7x08)">
            Attached
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard demonstrated command abilities early in his career, in particular, when he led an
          <a href="/wiki/Away_team" title="Away team">
           away team
          </a>
          on
          <a href="/wiki/Milika_III" title="Milika III">
           Milika III
          </a>
          to save an
          <a href="/wiki/Ambassador" title="Ambassador">
           ambassador
          </a>
          . This incident would later be mentioned by Q as one of the crucial events forming Picard's personality. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          As a young
          <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant" title="Lieutenant">
           lieutenant
          </a>
          , Picard attended the
          <a href="/wiki/Wedding" title="Wedding">
           wedding
          </a>
          of
          <a href="/wiki/Sarek" title="Sarek">
           Sarek
          </a>
          's son, where he briefly met Sarek and
          <a href="/wiki/Spock" title="Spock">
           Spock
          </a>
          for the first and only time before the
          <a href="/wiki/2360s" title="2360s">
           2360s
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Sarek_(episode)" title="Sarek (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Sarek (TNG 3x23)">
            Sarek
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Unification_I_(episode)" title="Unification I (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Unification I (TNG 5x07)">
            Unification I
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           Caution was still in place during the writing of "
           <a href="/wiki/Sarek_(episode)" title="Sarek (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Sarek (TNG 3x23)">
             Sarek
            </span>
           </a>
           " about dealing with characters from
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Original_Series" title="Star Trek: The Original Series">
           The Original Series
          </a>
          <i>
           , thus it is only implied that the son in question is Spock. (
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation_Companion" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation Companion">
           Star Trek: The Next Generation Companion
          </a>
          <i>
           ) Picard's line in "
           <a href="/wiki/Unification_I_(episode)" title="Unification I (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Unification I (TNG 5x07)">
             Unification I
            </span>
           </a>
           " only states that he has met Spock before but does not explicitly state when that meeting occurred, though likely it would have been at the wedding. This wedding was portrayed in the early chapters of Josepha Sherman and Susan Shwartz's novel
           <a href="/wiki/Vulcan%27s_Heart" title="Vulcan's Heart">
            Vulcan's Heart
           </a>
           .
          </i>
         </div>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Aboard_the_Stargazer">
           Aboard the
           <i>
            Stargazer
           </i>
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit Aboard the Stargazer section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/8/8a/Picard_stargazer_command_chair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120821235345&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard stargazer command chair" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_stargazer_command_chair.jpg" data-image-name="Picard stargazer command chair.jpg" data-src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/8/8a/Picard_stargazer_command_chair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120821235345&amp;path-prefix=en" height="135" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard stargazer command chair" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_stargazer_command_chair.jpg" data-image-name="Picard stargazer command chair.jpg" height="135" src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/8/8a/Picard_stargazer_command_chair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120821235345&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_stargazer_command_chair.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard on the bridge of the
            <i>
             Stargazer
            </i>
            some years after its loss
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Picard was assigned as a
          <a href="/wiki/Flight_controller" title="Flight controller">
           flight controller
          </a>
          aboard the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Stargazer" title="USS Stargazer">
           USS
           <i>
            Stargazer
           </i>
          </a>
          . In
          <a href="/wiki/2333" title="2333">
           2333
          </a>
          , as a
          <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant_commander" title="Lieutenant commander">
           lieutenant commander
          </a>
          , he assumed command of the vessel when the
          <a href="/wiki/Captain" title="Captain">
           captain
          </a>
          was killed on the
          <a href="/wiki/Bridge" title="Bridge">
           bridge
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Battle_(episode)" title="The Battle (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Battle (TNG 1x09)">
            The Battle
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Relics_(episode)" title="Relics (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Relics (TNG 6x04)">
            Relics
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Bloodlines_(episode)" title="Bloodlines (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Bloodlines (TNG 7x22)">
            Bloodlines
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet" title="Starfleet">
           Starfleet
          </a>
          awarded Picard a promotion to the post of captain, making him one of the youngest Starfleet officers ever to attain the position. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Picard remained in command of the
          <i>
           Stargazer
          </i>
          for twenty-two years. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Battle_(episode)" title="The Battle (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Battle (TNG 1x09)">
            The Battle
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           It is unlikely Picard was promoted directly to the rank of captain as he was assigned command of
          </i>
          Stargazer
          <i>
           , but more likely to the rank of commander before being promoted to the higher grade later. In accordance with naval rank tradition, one does not have to hold a captain's rank to command a vessel (most were actually commanded by officers holding the rank of commander), and anyone who is commanding is called 'Captain' regardless of rank.
           <div style="margin-top:.5em">
            Also while not explicitly mentioned, it is implied during
            <a href="/wiki/William_T._Riker" title="William T. Riker">
             Cmdr. Riker
            </a>
            's first meeting with him that Picard had previously served as a first officer before being promoted to Captain, a position he would have served simultaneously to serving as the flight controller of the Stargazer
            <i>
             .
            </i>
           </div>
           <div style="margin-top:.5em">
            The length of Picard's command of the Stargazer
            <i>
             is from the
            </i>
            Star Trek: The Next Generation Writers'/Directors' Guide
            <i>
             . The year he took command is derived from "
             <a href="/wiki/The_Battle_(episode)" title="The Battle (episode)">
              <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Battle (TNG 1x09)">
               The Battle
              </span>
             </a>
             ", in which it is stated Picard lost the
            </i>
            Stargazer
            <i>
             in
             <a href="/wiki/2355" title="2355">
              2355
             </a>
             .
            </i>
           </div>
          </i>
         </div>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2342" title="2342">
           2342
          </a>
          , Picard dated a young woman named
          <a href="/wiki/Jenice_Manheim" title="Jenice Manheim">
           Jenice
          </a>
          at the
          <a href="/wiki/Caf%C3%A9_des_Artistes" title="Caf des Artistes">
           Caf des Artistes
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">
           Paris
          </a>
          . However, he became afraid of a possible future relationship and posted Jenice, who later married
          <a href="/wiki/Paul_Manheim" title="Paul Manheim">
           Paul Manheim
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/We%27ll_Always_Have_Paris_(episode)" title="We'll Always Have Paris (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="We'll Always Have Paris (TNG 1x24)">
            We'll Always Have Paris
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          During the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cardassian_wars" title="Cardassian wars">
           Cardassian wars
          </a>
          , the
          <i>
           Stargazer
          </i>
          was involved in a truce offering by the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">
           Federation
          </a>
          . After making contact with a
          <a href="/wiki/Cardassian" title="Cardassian">
           Cardassian
          </a>
          warship, Picard lowered the ship's
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shields" title="Shields">
           shields
          </a>
          as a gesture of good will, but the Cardassian commander ignored the gesture and disabled the
          <i>
           Stargazer
          </i>
          's
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Weapon" title="Weapon">
           weapons
          </a>
          and
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Impulse_engine" title="Impulse engine">
           impulse engines
          </a>
          . The
          <i>
           Stargazer
          </i>
          managed to regroup and flee. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Wounded_(episode)" title="The Wounded (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Wounded (TNG 4x12)">
            The Wounded
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/0/0c/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2350s.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120111003558&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, 2350s" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2350s.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, 2350s.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/0/0c/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2350s.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120111003558&amp;path-prefix=en" height="177" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>

            <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, 2350s" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2350s.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, 2350s.jpg" height="177" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/0/0c/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2350s.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120111003558&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>

         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2354" title="2354">
           2354
          </a>
          , Picard was on an
          <a href="/wiki/Away_mission" title="Away mission">
           away mission
          </a>
          when he saved the life of one team member at the expense of another;
          <a href="/wiki/Jack_Crusher" title="Jack Crusher">
           Jack Crusher
          </a>
          was lost in the line of duty. Picard met with Crusher's widow,
          <a href="/wiki/Beverly_Crusher" title="Beverly Crusher">
           Beverly
          </a>
          , on
          <a href="/wiki/Starbase_32" title="Starbase 32">
           Starbase 32
          </a>
          to present the body; it was one of
          <a href="/wiki/Wesley_Crusher" title="Wesley Crusher">
           Wesley Crusher
          </a>
          's earliest memories. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Encounter_at_Farpoint_(episode)" title="Encounter at Farpoint (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Encounter at Farpoint (TNG 1x01/02)">
            Encounter at Farpoint
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Coming_of_Age_(episode)" title="Coming of Age (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Coming of Age (TNG 1x19)">
            Coming of Age
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Bonding_(episode)" title="The Bonding (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Bonding (TNG 3x05)">
            The Bonding
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Violations_(episode)" title="Violations (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Violations (TNG 5x12)">
            Violations
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2355" title="2355">
           2355
          </a>
          , the
          <i>
           Stargazer
          </i>
          was seriously damaged in a battle with an unknown enemy vessel, later discovered to be a
          <a href="/wiki/Ferengi" title="Ferengi">
           Ferengi
          </a>
          ship. Picard managed to destroy the enemy vessel using the
          <i>
           Stargazer
          </i>
          's
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Warp_engine" title="Warp engine">
           warp engines
          </a>
          in a unique tactical maneuver (later named the "
          <a href="/wiki/Picard_Maneuver" title="Picard Maneuver">
           Picard Maneuver
          </a>
          "), but was forced to abandon the
          <i>
           Stargazer
          </i>
          . His actions during the battle were called into question by Starfleet prosecutor
          <a href="/wiki/Phillipa_Louvois" title="Phillipa Louvois">
           Phillipa Louvois
          </a>
          , but he was exonerated by the inquiry board and was later awarded the
          <a href="/wiki/Grankite_Order_of_Tactics" title="Grankite Order of Tactics">
           Grankite Order of Tactics (Class of Excellence)
          </a>
          for the development of the Picard Maneuver. The encounter with the Ferengi vessel, later known as the
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Maxia" title="Battle of Maxia">
           Battle of Maxia
          </a>
          , eventually came back to haunt Picard.
          <a href="/wiki/DaiMon" title="DaiMon">
           DaiMon
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Bok" title="Bok">
           Bok
          </a>
          , whose son was killed in the battle, twice tried to exact revenge on Picard. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Battle_(episode)" title="The Battle (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Battle (TNG 1x09)">
            The Battle
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Measure_Of_A_Man_(episode)" title="The Measure Of A Man (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Measure Of A Man (TNG 2x09)">
            The Measure Of A Man
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Bloodlines_(episode)" title="Bloodlines (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Bloodlines (TNG 7x22)">
            Bloodlines
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <a href="/wiki/Picard_family_album" title="Picard family album">
           Picard family album
          </a>
          from
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Generations" title="Star Trek Generations">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Generations">
             Star Trek Generations
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Captain_of_the_Enterprise">
           Captain of the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit Captain of the Enterprise section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/68/Picard_looking_out%2C_2364.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150413060348&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard looking out, 2364" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_looking_out%2C_2364.jpg" data-image-name="Picard looking out, 2364.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/68/Picard_looking_out%2C_2364.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150413060348&amp;path-prefix=en" height="164" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard looking out, 2364" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_looking_out%2C_2364.jpg" data-image-name="Picard looking out, 2364.jpg" height="164" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/68/Picard_looking_out%2C_2364.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150413060348&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_looking_out,_2364.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard, shortly after taking command of the
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
           2364
          </a>
          , Picard was assigned command of the newly commissioned
          <a href="/wiki/Galaxy_class" title="Galaxy class">
           <i>
            Galaxy
           </i>
           -class
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Starship" title="Starship">
           starship
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-D)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-D)">
           USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -D
          </a>
          , the most prestigious captaincy in
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet" title="Starfleet">
           Starfleet
          </a>
          . He commanded the flagship for seven years, participating in many important missions. Among these were the defeat of the
          <a href="/wiki/Borg" title="Borg">
           Borg
          </a>
          invasions of
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          , and his command of the fleet which blockaded the
          <a href="/wiki/Klingon-Romulan_border" title="Klingon-Romulan border">
           Klingon-Romulan border
          </a>
          during the
          <a href="/wiki/Klingon_Civil_War" title="Klingon Civil War">
           Klingon Civil War
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/43/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_early_2364.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120205053315&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, early 2364" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_early_2364.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, early 2364.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/43/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_early_2364.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120205053315&amp;path-prefix=en" height="135" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, early 2364" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_early_2364.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, early 2364.jpg" height="135" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/43/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_early_2364.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120205053315&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean-Luc_Picard,_early_2364.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            "
            <i>
             Let's see what's out there...
            </i>
            "
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           What Picard did for the nine years between the
          </i>
          Stargazer
          <i>
           and the
          </i>
          Enterprise
          <i>
           is unknown and has never been discussed in any
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek" title="Star Trek">
           Star Trek
          </a>
          <i>
           production. The amount of time would have been sufficient for him to command another starship, but Picard has never mentioned another starship command beside the
          </i>
          Stargazer
          <i>
           and
          </i>
          Enterprise
          <i>
           . The novel
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/The_Buried_Age" title="The Buried Age">
           The Buried Age
          </a>
          <i>
           filled in many of the gaps, including Picard's first meetings with Troi,
           <a href="/wiki/Data" title="Data">
            Data
           </a>
           , Yar,
           <a href="/wiki/Kathryn_Janeway" title="Kathryn Janeway">
            Kathryn Janeway
           </a>
           , and La Forge.
           <div style="margin-top:.5em">
            In the
            <a href="/wiki/TNG_Season_4" title="TNG Season 4">
             fourth season
            </a>
            episode "
            <a href="/wiki/Legacy_(episode)" title="Legacy (episode)">
             <span style="cursor: help;" title="Legacy (TNG 4x06)">
              Legacy
             </span>
            </a>
            ", when Picard talked to Ishara Yar in sickbay, he related that he first met Tasha when Picard's ship and the ship that Tasha was assigned to at the time responded to a distress call and Tasha was on the planet's surface saving wounded colonists. Since Tasha was on the Enterprise
            <i>
             when the ship left Spacedock for its first mission, it would appear that Picard was commanding another ship when he met Tasha.
            </i>
           </div>
          </i>
         </div>
         <p>
          Picard hand-picked most of his
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senior_staff" title="Senior staff">
           senior staff
          </a>
          , such as two young officers who impressed him enough upon first meeting.
          <a href="/wiki/Geordi_La_Forge" title="Geordi La Forge">
           Geordi La Forge
          </a>
          once piloted Picard's inspection tour shuttle and stayed up all night to
          <a href="/wiki/Refit" title="Refit">
           refit
          </a>
          an engine part Picard had made a passing comment on, and Picard witnessed
          <a href="/wiki/Natasha_Yar" title="Natasha Yar">
           Natasha Yar
          </a>
          risk her life to save colonists amid a
          <a href="/wiki/Carnelian_minefield" title="Carnelian minefield">
           Carnelian minefield
          </a>
          . He had also picked
          <a href="/wiki/William_T._Riker" title="William T. Riker">
           William T. Riker
          </a>
          as his
          <a href="/wiki/First_officer" title="First officer">
           first officer
          </a>
          and promoted him to
          <a href="/wiki/Commander" title="Commander">
           commander
          </a>
          sight unseen, impressed by the young officer's record of independence. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Next_Phase_(episode)" title="The Next Phase (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Next Phase (TNG 5x24)">
            The Next Phase
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Legacy_(episode)" title="Legacy (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Legacy (TNG 4x06)">
            Legacy
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Pegasus_(episode)" title="The Pegasus (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Pegasus (TNG 7x12)">
            The Pegasus
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Mere months after taking command, Picard was offered a promotion to commandant of
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet_Academy" title="Starfleet Academy">
           Starfleet Academy
          </a>
          with the rank of
          <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">
           admiral
          </a>
          by Admiral
          <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Quinn" title="Gregory Quinn">
           Gregory Quinn
          </a>
          , but turned it down to retain command of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Coming_of_Age_(episode)" title="Coming of Age (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Coming of Age (TNG 1x19)">
            Coming of Age
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/cf/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2370.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120921121037&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, 2370" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2370.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, 2370.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/cf/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2370.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120921121037&amp;path-prefix=en" height="162" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, 2370" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2370.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, 2370.jpg" height="162" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/cf/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2370.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120921121037&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean-Luc_Picard,_2370.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard on the bridge of the
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
            in 2370
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Although Picard often heatedly defended a strict interpretation of the
          <a href="/wiki/Prime_Directive" title="Prime Directive">
           Prime Directive
          </a>
          , he broke it numerous times when he felt it was warranted. Thus, in 2364, he allowed an
          <a href="/wiki/Edo" title="Edo">
           Edo
          </a>
          woman to confront her "god" from space, and in
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , Picard brought a
          <a href="/wiki/Mintakan" title="Mintakan">
           Mintakan
          </a>
          leader aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          so as to undo the damage done by
          <a href="/wiki/Cultural_contamination" title="Cultural contamination">
           cultural contamination
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Justice_(episode)" title="Justice (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Justice (TNG 1x08)">
            Justice
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Who_Watches_The_Watchers_(episode)" title="Who Watches The Watchers (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Who Watches The Watchers (TNG 3x04)">
            Who Watches The Watchers
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Drumhead_(episode)" title="The Drumhead (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Drumhead (TNG 4x21)">
            The Drumhead
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Furthermore, in
          <a href="/wiki/2370" title="2370">
           2370
          </a>
          , the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , by hand of Dr.
          <a href="/wiki/Nikolai_Rozhenko" title="Nikolai Rozhenko">
           Nikolai Rozhenko
          </a>
          , transported a primitive group of
          <a href="/wiki/Boraalan" title="Boraalan">
           Boraalans
          </a>
          aboard from
          <a href="/wiki/Boraal_II" title="Boraal II">
           Boraal II
          </a>
          before an
          <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_dissipation" title="Atmospheric dissipation">
           atmospheric dissipation
          </a>
          rendered it uninhabitable. Although in violation of the Prime Directive, Picard ordered that the Boraalans be resettled. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Homeward_(episode)" title="Homeward (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Homeward (TNG 7x13)">
            Homeward
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In 2369, when the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          was undergoing a
          <a href="/wiki/Baryon_sweep" title="Baryon sweep">
           baryon sweep
          </a>
          at the
          <a href="/wiki/Remmler_Array" title="Remmler Array">
           Remmler Array
          </a>
          , Picard uncovered a plan, by mercenaries, to steal toxic waste from the ship's
          <a href="/wiki/Warp_core" title="Warp core">
           warp core
          </a>
          . He managed to take out all of the intruders by setting traps throughout the various sections of the ship. He even used the
          <a href="/wiki/Vulcan_nerve_pinch" title="Vulcan nerve pinch">
           Vulcan nerve pinch
          </a>
          technique on one of them. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
