            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Starship_Mine_(episode)" title="Starship Mine (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Starship Mine (TNG 6x18)">
            Starship Mine
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Encounters_with_the_Q_entity">
           Encounters with the Q entity
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit Encounters with the Q entity section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          Commanding the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          on her first mission, Picard made first contact with a member of the
          <a href="/wiki/Q_Continuum" title="Q Continuum">
           Q Continuum
          </a>
          
          <a href="/wiki/Q" title="Q">
           Q
          </a>
          . Picard and his senior officers had to stand trial for
          <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">
           Humanity
          </a>
          's immaturity. To prove their worthiness as a species, Picard had to solve the "mystery of
          <a href="/wiki/Farpoint_Station" title="Farpoint Station">
           Farpoint Station
          </a>
          ." The crew of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          discovered that the inhabitants of
          <a href="/wiki/Deneb_IV" title="Deneb IV">
           Deneb IV
          </a>
          , the
          <a href="/wiki/Bandi" title="Bandi">
           Bandi
          </a>
          , had captured a space-dwelling being to serve their own purpose. The
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          helped to free the creature, and Q, somewhat disappointed by the crew's success, retreated, though he hinted that it would not be their final encounter. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Encounter_at_Farpoint_(episode)" title="Encounter at Farpoint (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Encounter at Farpoint (TNG 1x01/02)">
            Encounter at Farpoint
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/d/d2/Picard_Q_Ready_Room.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120820020531&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard Q Ready Room" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_Q_Ready_Room.jpg" data-image-name="Picard Q Ready Room.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/d/d2/Picard_Q_Ready_Room.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120820020531&amp;path-prefix=en" height="135" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard Q Ready Room" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_Q_Ready_Room.jpg" data-image-name="Picard Q Ready Room.jpg" height="135" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/d/d2/Picard_Q_Ready_Room.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120820020531&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_Q_Ready_Room.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Q explains to Picard that how Humans respond to a game tells him more about them than a direct confrontation would
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Thus, later that year, Q created a bizarre and deadly "game" for the crew of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          in order to demonstrate that he had given Riker Q-like abilities. Ultimately, Riker rejected these new powers, and Q again disappeared. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Hide_and_Q_(episode)" title="Hide and Q (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Hide and Q (TNG 1x10)">
            Hide and Q
           </span>
          </a>
          ") One year later, in
          <a href="/wiki/2365" title="2365">
           2365
          </a>
          , Q first expressed an interest in joining Picard's crew. When Picard declined, Q tried to show how much he could be of assistance by hurling the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          into the path of a
          <a href="/wiki/Borg_cube" title="Borg cube">
           Borg cube
          </a>
          . Q was hoping to show that the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">
           Federation
          </a>
          was entirely unprepared to meet some of the more powerful races that existed in the universe. Ultimately, Picard had to beg for Q's help in escaping from the pursuit of the
          <a href="/wiki/Borg" title="Borg">
           Borg
          </a>
          vessel. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Q_Who_(episode)" title="Q Who (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Q Who (TNG 2x16)">
            Q Who
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          A fourth encounter with Q occurred in
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , when the other members of the Continuum had stripped him of his omnipotence and immortality as punishment for his irresponsibility. He sought refuge on the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          and, although Picard and the rest of the crew were initially unconvinced of the sincerity of Q's pleas, the captain agreed to provide Q temporary asylum. As the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          began to suffer from
          <a href="/wiki/Calamarain" title="Calamarain">
           Calamarain
          </a>
          attack, however, Q resolved to end his life in order to prevent further risk to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          crew, but another member of the Q Continuum prevented Q from sacrificing himself, and restored his powers as a reward for his selfless act. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Deja_Q_(episode)" title="Deja Q (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Deja Q (TNG 3x13)">
            Deja Q
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Late in
          <a href="/wiki/2367" title="2367">
           2367
          </a>
          , Q returned to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          to "properly" thank Picard for his role in helping him regain his standing in the Continuum. At the time, Picard was meeting
          <a href="/wiki/Vash" title="Vash">
           Vash
          </a>
          , whom he had met on
          <a href="/wiki/Risa" title="Risa">
           Risa
          </a>
          the year before. Q resolved to teach Picard a lesson about love and cast the captain, Vash, and the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          command crew into an elaborate scenario styled by the ancient legend of
          <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
           Robin Hood
          </a>
          . Q himself assumed the role of the
          <a href="/wiki/Sheriff_of_Nottingham" title="Sheriff of Nottingham">
           Sheriff of Nottingham
          </a>
          . Ultimately, Picard learned his lesson, and everyone was returned to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . Intrigued by Vash, though, Q offered to take her on a journey of exploration to explore various archaeological ruins of the
          <a href="/wiki/Milky_Way_Galaxy" title="Milky Way Galaxy">
           galaxy
          </a>
          , and she accepted. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Qpid_(episode)" title="Qpid (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Qpid (TNG 4x20)">
            Qpid
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          , Q once again appeared aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , this time to instruct
          <a href="/wiki/Amanda_Rogers" title="Amanda Rogers">
           Amanda Rogers
          </a>
          , a Human who was the child of two Q and possessed Q powers herself. Although Q's petulant and acerbic attitude did little to ingratiate himself to Amanda, he eventually convinced her to go with him to the Continuum to learn to use her new-found abilities. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/True_Q_(episode)" title="True Q (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="True Q (TNG 6x06)">
            True Q
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Later that same year, Q appeared to Picard when the latter was critically injured in a
          <a href="/wiki/Lenarian" title="Lenarian">
           Lenarian
          </a>
          ambush. Appearing as "
          <a href="/wiki/God" title="God">
           God
          </a>
          ", Q told Picard that he had died because of his
          <a href="/wiki/Artificial_heart" title="Artificial heart">
           artificial heart
          </a>
          , and offered him the chance to return to the incident in his youth, allowing him to relive the events leading up to his near-fatal injury and change history. Although Picard was successful in changing history, he eventually realized that the event  and his previous nature as an arrogant, brash young man  was a part of his identity, and had helped mold him into the successful
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet" title="Starfleet">
           Starfleet
          </a>
          officer he had become. Although he was uncertain as to whether the experience had been real or simply a vision, Picard was grateful for Q's revelation. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/14/Q_and_Picard%2C_2370.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120920171127&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Q and Picard, 2370" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Q_and_Picard%2C_2370.jpg" data-image-name="Q and Picard, 2370.jpg" data-src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/14/Q_and_Picard%2C_2370.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120920171127&amp;path-prefix=en" height="140" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Q and Picard, 2370" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Q_and_Picard%2C_2370.jpg" data-image-name="Q and Picard, 2370.jpg" height="140" src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/14/Q_and_Picard%2C_2370.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120920171127&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Q_and_Picard,_2370.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            "
            <i>
             You don't get it, do you, Jean-Luc? The trial never ends.
            </i>
            "
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2370" title="2370">
           2370
          </a>
          , Q returned to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          to continue the trial against Humanity. Claiming that the seven-year-old trial had never actually ended, Q proclaimed Humanity guilty of "being inferior" and informed Picard that his race was to be destroyed. He sent Picard traveling through time to his past, present, and future, where he was presented with a
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Temporal_paradox" title="Temporal paradox">
           temporal paradox
          </a>
          in the form of an eruption of
          <a href="/wiki/Anti-time" title="Anti-time">
           anti-time
          </a>
          in the
          <a href="/wiki/Devron_system" title="Devron system">
           Devron system
          </a>
          . In this paradox, Picard himself was responsible for the creation of the anomaly that propagated backwards in normal time (anti-time having the opposite properties of normal time), thus destroying Humanity in the past.
         </p>
         <p>
          However, in addition to sending Picard jumping through time, Q also provided Picard with hints to understanding the nature of the paradox. Ultimately, Picard determined the solution and devised a way to close the anti-time anomaly in all three time periods. Following the captain's success, Q revealed that the entire experience had been a test, aimed at determining whether Humanity was capable of expanding its horizons to understand some of the advanced concepts of the universe. Departing, Q promised to continue watching Humanity, proclaiming that "The trial never ends." (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/All_Good_Things..._(episode)" title="All Good Things... (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="All Good Things... (TNG 7x25/26)">
            All Good Things...
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Encounters_with_the_Borg">
           Encounters with the Borg
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit Encounters with the Borg section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/6a/Picard_kidnapped_by_the_Borg.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130423000049&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard kidnapped by the Borg" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_kidnapped_by_the_Borg.jpg" data-image-name="Picard kidnapped by the Borg.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/6a/Picard_kidnapped_by_the_Borg.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130423000049&amp;path-prefix=en" height="156" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard kidnapped by the Borg" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_kidnapped_by_the_Borg.jpg" data-image-name="Picard kidnapped by the Borg.jpg" height="156" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/6a/Picard_kidnapped_by_the_Borg.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130423000049&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_kidnapped_by_the_Borg.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Abducted by the Borg in 2366
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2365" title="2365">
           2365
          </a>
          , Q sent the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          7,000
          <a href="/wiki/Light_year" title="Light year">
           light years
          </a>
          into uncharted space, into the path of a
          <a href="/wiki/Borg_cube" title="Borg cube">
           Borg cube
          </a>
          . Although the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          suffered losses, it became the first ship known by the Federation to survive an encounter with the
          <a href="/wiki/Borg" title="Borg">
           Borg
          </a>
          and so managed to inform Starfleet of the Borg's existence. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Q_Who_(episode)" title="Q Who (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Q Who (TNG 2x16)">
            Q Who
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          One year later, in
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , the Borg launched their first invasion of the Federation. A single cube destroyed the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Providence" title="New Providence">
           New Providence
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Colony" title="Colony">
           colony
          </a>
          and the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Lalo" title="USS Lalo">
           USS
           <i>
            Lalo
           </i>
          </a>
          , and kidnapped Picard when the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          attempted to intervene. Picard was partially
          <a href="/wiki/Assimilation" title="Assimilation">
           assimilated
          </a>
          and became a
          <a href="/wiki/Borg_drone" title="Borg drone">
           Borg drone
          </a>
          known as
          <a href="/wiki/Locutus_of_Borg" title="Locutus of Borg">
           Locutus of Borg
          </a>
          . The cube proceeded towards
          <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">
           Earth
          </a>
          and engaged Starfleet in the
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Wolf_359" title="Battle of Wolf 359">
           Battle of Wolf 359
          </a>
          , resulting in the destruction of 39 Federation vessels. On arrival at Earth, an
          <a href="/wiki/Away_team" title="Away team">
           away team
          </a>
          from the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          successfully rescued Picard and used his connection to the Borg to implant false data in the cube, destroying it. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds (TNG 3x26)">
            The Best of Both Worlds
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds,_Part_II_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (TNG 4x01)">
            The Best of Both Worlds, Part II
           </span>
          </a>
          ") It was revealed years later that his assimilation and time spent in the
          <a href="/wiki/Borg_Collective" title="Borg Collective">
           Collective
          </a>
          had a profoundly disturbing effect on Picard's life. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/64/Locutus_of_Borg_and_Borg_Queen.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100810174835&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Locutus of Borg and Borg Queen" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Locutus_of_Borg_and_Borg_Queen.jpg" data-image-name="Locutus of Borg and Borg Queen.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/64/Locutus_of_Borg_and_Borg_Queen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100810174835&amp;path-prefix=en" height="110" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Locutus of Borg and Borg Queen" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Locutus_of_Borg_and_Borg_Queen.jpg" data-image-name="Locutus of Borg and Borg Queen.jpg" height="110" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/64/Locutus_of_Borg_and_Borg_Queen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100810174835&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Locutus_of_Borg_and_Borg_Queen.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard as Locutus of Borg, and the Borg Queen
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          again encountered the Borg in
          <a href="/wiki/2368" title="2368">
           2368
          </a>
          when they rescued a Borg drone from a crashed Borg shuttle. This drone was cut off from the Collective and slowly regained an individual identity, eventually being named
          <a href="/wiki/Hugh" title="Hugh">
           Hugh
          </a>
          . Initially, the plan was drafted to use Hugh to destroy the collective in its entirety, although Dr.
          <a href="/wiki/Beverly_Crusher" title="Beverly Crusher">
           Beverly Crusher
          </a>
          resisted the extermination of an entire race  even if it was the Borg. Picard eventually confronted Hugh, who immediately recognized Picard as Locutus. Picard took the role of Locutus while talking to Hugh, to simulate the authority that Hugh was used to. However, Geordi La Forge,
          <a href="/wiki/Data" title="Data">
           Data
          </a>
          , Dr. Crusher, and other members of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          crew had a profound effect on the former drone. Even
          <a href="/wiki/Guinan" title="Guinan">
           Guinan
          </a>
          , who initially wanted nothing to do with Hugh, taught him that resistance is not futile. Guinan's homeworld had been destroyed long ago by the Borg, but the fact that Guinan was still alive was proof of this assertion.
         </p>
         <p>
          When Picard reminded Hugh that "resistance is futile," Hugh informed him that it was not so. When Picard told Hugh that La Forge would be assimilated, Hugh stated that La Forge did not want to be assimilated. When Picard said that this was irrelevant, Hugh specifically said that he (and Hugh used the word "I") would not assist in the assimilation of La Forge. Picard was stunned that a Borg drone would say such things. He decided that he could not send Hugh back with the file that would destroy the Borg. Picard offered Hugh asylum on board the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , but Hugh said that the Collective would not stop looking for him until they found him. Hugh agreed to go back to the crash site and to be taken back into the Collective, to protect the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          from harm. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/I_Borg_(episode)" title="I Borg (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="I Borg (TNG 5x23)">
            I Borg
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          The individuality present in Hugh spread through the ship he returned to, causing a catastrophic separation of the ship from the rest of the Collective. This rogue mini-collective was unsure how to cope with its freedom, and so fell under the influence of the android
          <a href="/wiki/Lore" title="Lore">
           Lore
          </a>
          . Lore persuaded them to aid his plan to conquer Earth. Using the
          <a href="/wiki/Borg_Type_03" title="Borg Type 03">
           rogue ship
          </a>
          , they attacked several outposts before being tracked down by the crew of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -D. They destroyed the Borg ship and were able to persuade the remaining members of the mini-collective of Lore's unreliability. The mini-collective then disappeared into space and has not been encountered since. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Descent_(episode)" title="Descent (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Descent (TNG 6x26)">
            Descent
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Descent,_Part_II_(episode)" title="Descent, Part II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Descent, Part II (TNG 7x01)">
            Descent, Part II
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          There were some within Starfleet who blamed Picard for the destruction of the task force at
          <a href="/wiki/Wolf_359" title="Wolf 359">
           Wolf 359
          </a>
          .
          <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Sisko" title="Benjamin Sisko">
           Benjamin Sisko
          </a>
          , who was serving as
          <a href="/wiki/First_officer" title="First officer">
           first officer
          </a>
          of the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Saratoga_(NCC-31911)" title="USS Saratoga (NCC-31911)">
           USS
           <i>
            Saratoga
           </i>
          </a>
          at the time, lost his wife
          <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Sisko" title="Jennifer Sisko">
           Jennifer
          </a>
          in the attack. Picard and Sisko finally met in
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          , after the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          was the first Starfleet vessel to arrive at
          <a href="/wiki/Deep_Space_9" title="Deep Space 9">
           Deep Space 9
          </a>
          . Sisko was, at first, hostile toward Picard, but later came to forgive him. Sisko also gave Picard his letter of resignation, which Picard did not send, feeling Sisko was the right person for command of Deep Space 9. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
            DS9
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Emissary_(episode)" title="Emissary (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Emissary (DS9 1x01/02)">
            Emissary
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/2/2c/Welcome_home_Locutus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070614024929&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Welcome home Locutus" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Welcome_home_Locutus.jpg" data-image-name="Welcome home Locutus.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/2/2c/Welcome_home_Locutus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070614024929&amp;path-prefix=en" height="76" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Welcome home Locutus" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Welcome_home_Locutus.jpg" data-image-name="Welcome home Locutus.jpg" height="76" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/2/2c/Welcome_home_Locutus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070614024929&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Welcome_home_Locutus.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Meeting the Borg Queen again
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2373" title="2373">
           2373
          </a>
          , the Borg launched their second invasion of the Federation, and again the crew of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          played a major role in their defeat. Initially, the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          was not to have participated in the
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Sector_001" title="Battle of Sector 001">
           Battle of Sector 001
          </a>
          , because according to
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet_Command" title="Starfleet Command">
           Starfleet Command
          </a>
          , Picard would bring an "unstable element into a critical situation." Seeing that the Borg were getting the best of the fleet, Picard ordered the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          to Earth to assist. He was instrumental in defeating both the main invasion and an attempt by the Borg to prevent the formation of the Federation by altering history. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Kamin_and_the_Ressikan_Probe">
           Kamin and the Ressikan Probe
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit Kamin and the Ressikan Probe section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/5/5c/Picard_playing_Ressikan_Flute.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120208015651&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard playing Ressikan Flute" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_playing_Ressikan_Flute.jpg" data-image-name="Picard playing Ressikan Flute.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/5/5c/Picard_playing_Ressikan_Flute.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120208015651&amp;path-prefix=en" height="135" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard playing Ressikan Flute" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_playing_Ressikan_Flute.jpg" data-image-name="Picard playing Ressikan Flute.jpg" height="135" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/5/5c/Picard_playing_Ressikan_Flute.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120208015651&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_playing_Ressikan_Flute.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard plays his Ressikan flute in private
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2368" title="2368">
           2368
          </a>
          , the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          encountered a space
          <a href="/wiki/Probe" title="Probe">
           probe
          </a>
          of unknown origin, which emitted a
          <a href="/wiki/Nucleonic_beam" title="Nucleonic beam">
           nucleonic beam
          </a>
          directly at Picard. This led to his fainting and awakening on an unknown world where he was known as an ironworker named
          <a href="/wiki/Kamin" title="Kamin">
           Kamin
          </a>
          and was married to
          <a href="/wiki/Eline" title="Eline">
           Eline
          </a>
          . Picard later found out that Kamin was a member of the
          <a href="/wiki/Ressik" title="Ressik">
           Ressik
          </a>
          community on a planet called
          <a href="/wiki/Kataan" title="Kataan">
           Kataan
          </a>
          . For five years, Picard clung to his life aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          and searched for ways to return, but eventually settled into his life as Kamin, having two children with Eline and eventually a grandchild. In the approximately 35 years Picard spent as Kamin, he learned to play the
          <a href="/wiki/Ressikan_flute" title="Ressikan flute">
           Ressikan flute
          </a>
          , dabbled in
          <a href="/wiki/Astronomy" title="Astronomy">
           astronomy
          </a>
          , and analyzed soil samples from the planet, eventually confirming that Kataan was a dying world.
         </p>
         <p>
          Near the end of his life on Kataan, it was revealed to Picard that Kataan had been destroyed more than 1,000 years previously, and the residents of the Ressik community had engineered the probe to share the memory and experiences of their people with someone who could then teach others about their civilization. He awoke on the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          as Jean-Luc Picard once more and discovered that he had lived a lifetime in only 25 minutes. The probe was collected by the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          and disassembled. A Ressikan flute was found inside the probe, which Riker then presented to Picard. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Inner_Light_(episode)" title="The Inner Light (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Inner Light (TNG 5x25)">
            The Inner Light
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard considered the flute to be one of his most prized possessions. As of
          <a href="/wiki/2379" title="2379">
           2379
          </a>
          , he kept the flute on his desk in his
          <a href="/wiki/Captain%27s_ready_room" title="Captain's ready room">
           ready room
          </a>
          aboard the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-E)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-E)">
           USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -E
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Lessons_(episode)" title="Lessons (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Lessons (TNG 6x19)">
            Lessons
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           <span class="audiolink">
            <a class="internal" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/66/RessikanFlute.ogg/revision/latest?cb=20040907040448&amp;path-prefix=en" title="RessikanFlute.ogg">
             Picard playing the Ressikan Flute
            </a>
           </span>
           <a href="/wiki/File:RessikanFlute.ogg" title="File:RessikanFlute.ogg">
            <sup>
             fileinfo
            </sup>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Later_career">
           Later career
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit Later career section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/6b/Picard_on_the_bridge_2373.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101012220140&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard on the bridge 2373" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_on_the_bridge_2373.jpg" data-image-name="Picard on the bridge 2373.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/6b/Picard_on_the_bridge_2373.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101012220140&amp;path-prefix=en" height="77" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard on the bridge 2373" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_on_the_bridge_2373.jpg" data-image-name="Picard on the bridge 2373.jpg" height="77" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/6b/Picard_on_the_bridge_2373.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101012220140&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_on_the_bridge_2373.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard in command of the
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
            -E
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2371" title="2371">
           2371
          </a>
          , the USS
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -D was lost over
          <a href="/wiki/Veridian_III" title="Veridian III">
           Veridian III
          </a>
          , with the vessel's
          <a href="/wiki/Primary_hull" title="Primary hull">
           primary hull
          </a>
          crash-landing on the planet's surface. Picard also met the legendary
          <a href="/wiki/James_T._Kirk" title="James T. Kirk">
           James T. Kirk
          </a>
          while in the
          <a href="/wiki/Nexus" title="Nexus">
           Nexus
          </a>
          with him, and recruited him in defeating and killing Dr.
          <a href="/wiki/Tolian_Soran" title="Tolian Soran">
           Tolian Soran
          </a>
          before he could have the chance to destroy the Veridian system. There were no fatalities aboard the Enterprise, and most of the ship's senior crew was reassigned to the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-E)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-E)">
           USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -E
          </a>
          , the sixth Federation starship to bear the name. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Generations" title="Star Trek Generations">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Generations">
             Star Trek Generations
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          ) Picard was installed as
          <a href="/wiki/Commanding_officer" title="Commanding officer">
           commanding officer
          </a>
          and given a new
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Authorization_code" title="Authorization code">
           authorization code
          </a>
          : "Picard-4-7-alpha-tango." After a one-year
          <a href="/wiki/Shakedown_cruise" title="Shakedown cruise">
           shakedown cruise
          </a>
          , the new
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          was nearly lost when the senior staff decided to sacrifice the ship in order to save
          <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">
           Earth
          </a>
          's future by preventing the Borg on board from changing history. Fortunately, the crew was able to repel the Borg attempt without having to destroy the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Two years later, in
          <a href="/wiki/2375" title="2375">
           2375
          </a>
          , Picard ordered the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E to the
          <a href="/wiki/Ba%27ku" title="Ba'ku">
           Ba'ku
          </a>
          homeworld in the
          <a href="/wiki/Briar_Patch" title="Briar Patch">
           Briar Patch
          </a>
          when it appeared that his
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Operations_manager" title="Operations manager">
           operations officer
          </a>
          ,
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lieutenant_Commander" title="Lieutenant Commander">
           Lieutenant Commander
          </a>
          Data, had malfunctioned and assaulted members of the research team there. Picard was able to capture Data and uncovered a plot by Admiral
          <a href="/wiki/Matthew_Dougherty" title="Matthew Dougherty">
           Matthew Dougherty
          </a>
          , the
          <a href="/wiki/Son%27a" title="Son'a">
           Son'a
          </a>
          and some in the
          <a href="/wiki/Federation_Council" title="Federation Council">
           Federation Council
          </a>
          to relocate the Ba'ku against their will. Picard rebelled against Dougherty, bringing word of his actions to the public. Picard was able to protect the Ba'ku and stop Son'a leader
          <a href="/wiki/Ru%27afo" title="Ru'afo">
           Ru'afo
          </a>
          from destroying the Ba'ku's homeworld. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Insurrection" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
             Star Trek: Insurrection
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/e/e0/Picard_and_Shinzon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100529010011&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard and Shinzon" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_and_Shinzon.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Shinzon.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/e/e0/Picard_and_Shinzon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100529010011&amp;path-prefix=en" height="76" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard and Shinzon" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_and_Shinzon.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Shinzon.jpg" height="76" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/e/e0/Picard_and_Shinzon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100529010011&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_and_Shinzon.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard and a dying Shinzon
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Picard continued in command of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          through
          <a href="/wiki/2379" title="2379">
           2379
          </a>
          , when the ship was sent to
          <a href="/wiki/Romulus" title="Romulus">
           Romulus
          </a>
          after the
          <i>
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coup" title="Coup">
            coup
           </a>
          </i>
          by
          <a href="/wiki/Praetor" title="Praetor">
           Praetor
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Shinzon" title="Shinzon">
           Shinzon
          </a>
          . Shinzon was a
          <a href="/wiki/Clone" title="Clone">
           clone
          </a>
          of Picard created by a former
          <a href="/wiki/Romulan" title="Romulan">
           Romulan
          </a>
          government  they intended to replace the captain with a spy of their own. Following a change of government and concern that it would lead to war, the plan was abandoned and Shinzon was sent to
          <a href="/wiki/Remus" title="Remus">
           Remus
          </a>
          to die. Instead, he prospered, becoming a highly successful leader during the
          <a href="/wiki/Dominion_War" title="Dominion War">
           Dominion War
          </a>
          . Shinzon used a
          <a href="/wiki/Thalaron_radiation" title="Thalaron radiation">
           thalaron radiation
          </a>
          weapon to eradicate the
          <a href="/wiki/Romulan_Senate" title="Romulan Senate">
           Romulan Senate
          </a>
          and had planned to do the same to Earth. He needed Picard in order to repair faults in his own genetic makeup.
         </p>
         <p>
          In a pitched battle between the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          and Shinzon's
          <a href="/wiki/Flagship" title="Flagship">
           flagship
          </a>
          , the
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Scimitar" title="Scimitar">
            Scimitar
           </a>
          </i>
          , Picard was eventually able to board the enemy ship and eliminate Shinzon. Data saved Picard's life by transporting the captain back to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          before sacrificing his own life; he destroyed the
          <i>
           Scimitar
          </i>
          by firing on the thalaron weapon with a hand
          <a href="/wiki/Phaser" title="Phaser">
           phaser
          </a>
          , thereby saving the over 800 men and women aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Medical_record">
           Medical record
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit Medical record section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p>
          Picard always remained in excellent health, thanks to a regimen carried over from his days as an athlete, and at the age of seventy-four (in 2379), was still a vibrant and healthy man. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Despite his captaincy of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , Picard still found time for
          <a href="/wiki/Fencing" title="Fencing">
           fencing
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Racquetball" title="Racquetball">
           racquetball
          </a>
          , and
          <a href="/wiki/Horse" title="Horse">
           equine
          </a>
          sports, usually on the
          <a href="/wiki/Holodeck" title="Holodeck">
           holodeck
          </a>
          . Nevertheless, he did show a tendency to overwork, avoided formal vacations, and had reported bouts of insomnia. Additionally, Picard usually tried to avoid his annual physicals, to the great irritation of Dr. Crusher. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/We%27ll_Always_Have_Paris_(episode)" title="We'll Always Have Paris (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="We'll Always Have Paris (TNG 1x24)">
            We'll Always Have Paris
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Pen_Pals_(episode)" title="Pen Pals (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Pen Pals (TNG 2x15)">
            Pen Pals
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Suddenly_Human_(episode)" title="Suddenly Human (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Suddenly Human (TNG 4x04)">
            Suddenly Human
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Captain%27s_Holiday_(episode)" title="Captain's Holiday (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Captain's Holiday (TNG 3x19)">
            Captain's Holiday
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Allegiance_(episode)" title="Allegiance (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Allegiance (TNG 3x18)">
            Allegiance
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          At a very young age, Picard was diagnosed with
          <a href="/wiki/Shalaft%27s_Syndrome" title="Shalaft's Syndrome">
           Shalaft's Syndrome
          </a>
          , a rare congenital defect that left him hypersensitive to any kind of sound. His condition was treated, but his hearing was still highly acute. As an ensign, Picard could sense subtleties as faint as a starship's torque sensors out of alignment by three microns. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Insurrection" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
             Star Trek: Insurrection
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          ;
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard lost his hair by the
          <a href="/wiki/2350s" title="2350s">
           2350s
          </a>
          , although he was known to have had a shaved head for some time as a student at
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet_Academy" title="Starfleet Academy">
           Starfleet Academy
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Rascals_(episode)" title="Rascals (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Rascals (TNG 6x07)">
            Rascals
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Violations_(episode)" title="Violations (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Violations (TNG 5x12)">
            Violations
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           Boothby's comment in
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/The_First_Duty_(episode)" title="The First Duty (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="The First Duty (TNG 5x19)">
             The First Duty
            </span>
           </a>
           ", by which he wondered what happened to Picard's hair, suggests that Picard did indeed have hair when they met. Picard also has thin brown hair when he is remembered by Beverly Crusher in "
           <a href="/wiki/Violations_(episode)" title="Violations (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Violations (TNG 5x12)">
             Violations
            </span>
           </a>
           ". However, both Shinzon and the photo of the younger Picard have clearly shaved heads.
          </i>
         </div>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/9f/Picard_during_surgery.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121208045415&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard during surgery" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_during_surgery.jpg" data-image-name="Picard during surgery.jpg" data-src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/9f/Picard_during_surgery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20121208045415&amp;path-prefix=en" height="134" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard during surgery" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_during_surgery.jpg" data-image-name="Picard during surgery.jpg" height="134" src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/9f/Picard_during_surgery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20121208045415&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_during_surgery.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Undergoing cardiac replacement surgery in 2365
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Owing to a near-fatal stabbing through the
          <a href="/wiki/Heart" title="Heart">
           heart
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/2328" title="2328">
           2328
          </a>
          , an
          <a href="/wiki/Artificial_heart" title="Artificial heart">
           artificial heart
          </a>
          was implanted to save Picard's life. The unit required replacement when it malfunctioned in
          <a href="/wiki/2365" title="2365">
           2365
          </a>
          , overseen at
          <a href="/wiki/Starbase_515" title="Starbase 515">
           Starbase 515
          </a>
          by Dr.
          <a href="/wiki/Katherine_Pulaski" title="Katherine Pulaski">
           Katherine Pulaski
          </a>
          . Four years later, the unit was damaged and again replaced following a near-fatal
          <a href="/wiki/Lenarian" title="Lenarian">
           Lenarian
          </a>
          compressed tetryon weaponry attack. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Samaritan_Snare_(episode)" title="Samaritan Snare (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Samaritan Snare (TNG 2x17)">
            Samaritan Snare
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Following his
          <a href="/wiki/Assimilation" title="Assimilation">
           assimilation
          </a>
          by the Borg in
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , Picard was formally declared dead as a casualty of war by Admiral
          <a href="/wiki/J.P._Hanson" title="J.P. Hanson">
           J.P. Hanson
          </a>
          . The ruling was rescinded six days later when Picard was recaptured by the crew of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . Along with the physical recovery, the invasive incident took an enormous emotional toll and required several weeks of counseling. Picard underwent similar, though less lengthy recuperation following his capture and torture by Cardassians in
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds (TNG 3x26)">
            The Best of Both Worlds
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Chain_of_Command,_Part_I_(episode)" title="Chain of Command, Part I (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Chain of Command, Part I (TNG 6x10)">
            Chain of Command, Part I
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Ronald_D._Moore" title="Ronald D. Moore">
            Ronald D. Moore
           </a>
           commented regarding Picard's assimilation: "
          </i>
          I lobbied for giving Picard a permanent
          <a href="/wiki/Biosynthetic_limb" title="Biosynthetic limb">
           bionic arm
          </a>
          , but
          <a href="/wiki/Rick_Berman" title="Rick Berman">
           Rick
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Michael_Piller" title="Michael Piller">
           Michael
          </a>
          wouldn't go for it. Picard's arm is his own.
          <i>
           " (
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Memory_Alpha:AOL_chats/Ronald_D._Moore/ron063.txt" title="Memory Alpha:AOL chats/Ronald D. Moore/ron063.txt">
           AOL chat
          </a>
          ,
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/1997_productions" title="1997 productions">
            1997
           </a>
           )
          </i>
         </div>
         <p>
          In an alternate future timeline, Jean-Luc developed
          <a href="/wiki/Irumodic_Syndrome" title="Irumodic Syndrome">
           Irumodic Syndrome
          </a>
          , and in the corresponding alternate "present" timeline in 2370 he became aware of his future condition due being shifted through time by
          <a href="/wiki/Q" title="Q">
           Q
          </a>
          .  Asking Dr. Crusher to perform medical scans on him in regards to this apparent fate, Crusher confirmed that Picard had a small structural defect that could possibly lead to Irumodic Syndrome, among other possible disorders. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/All_Good_Things..._(episode)" title="All Good Things... (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="All Good Things... (TNG 7x25/26)">
            All Good Things...
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           It is unclear whether this fact of Picard's health remained true after the restoration of the timeline apart from the Picard's experiences.
           <div style="margin-top:.5em">
            The
            <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine_-_Millennium" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine - Millennium">
             Star Trek: Deep Space Nine - Millennium
            </a>
            <i>
             novels depicted Picard with Irumodic Syndrome in 2400.
            </i>
           </div>
          </i>
         </div>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">
           Personal life
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit Personal life section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/44/Dixon_Hill.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120819032009&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Dixon Hill" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Dixon_Hill.jpg" data-image-name="Dixon Hill.jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/44/Dixon_Hill.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120819032009&amp;path-prefix=en" height="135" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Dixon Hill" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Dixon_Hill.jpg" data-image-name="Dixon Hill.jpg" height="135" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/44/Dixon_Hill.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120819032009&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Dixon_Hill.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard in a Dixon Hill holographic novel
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/f/f8/Picard_painting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091207012111&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard painting" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_painting.jpg" data-image-name="Picard painting.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/f/f8/Picard_painting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091207012111&amp;path-prefix=en" height="165" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard painting" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_painting.jpg" data-image-name="Picard painting.jpg" height="165" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/f/f8/Picard_painting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091207012111&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_painting.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard, while painting on the
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Picard held diverse intellectual interests and recreational pursuits. He was a lifelong avocational
          <a href="/wiki/Archaeologist" title="Archaeologist">
           archaeologist
          </a>
          , inspired by his Academy instructor, Richard Galen, having studied the
          <a href="/wiki/Iconian" title="Iconian">
           Iconian
          </a>
          culture since his cadet days. Picard even addressed the
          <a href="/wiki/Federation_Archaeology_Council" title="Federation Archaeology Council">
           Federation Archaeology Council
          </a>
          as keynote speaker in
          <a href="/wiki/2367" title="2367">
           2367
          </a>
          , on the subject of his oft-studied
          <a href="/wiki/Tagus_III" title="Tagus III">
           Tagus III
          </a>
          ruins. He also had a deep love of
          <a href="/wiki/Terran" title="Terran">
           Terran
          </a>
          literature, from the works of
          <a href="/wiki/William_Shakespeare" title="William Shakespeare">
           William Shakespeare
          </a>
          to detective stories featuring
          <a href="/wiki/Dixon_Hill" title="Dixon Hill">
           Dixon Hill
          </a>
          , and preferred to read them in their written form rather than on a holo-visual display. Picard had studied semantics and kept his
          <a href="/wiki/Latin" title="Latin">
           Latin
          </a>
          fresh. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Chase_(episode)" title="The Chase (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Chase (TNG 6x20)">
            The Chase
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Qpid_(episode)" title="Qpid (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Qpid (TNG 4x20)">
            Qpid
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Hide_and_Q_(episode)" title="Hide and Q (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Hide and Q (TNG 1x10)">
            Hide and Q
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Clues_(episode)" title="Clues (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Clues (TNG 4x14)">
            Clues
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Game_(episode)" title="The Game (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Game (TNG 5x06)">
            The Game
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Other subjects that enthralled Picard were
          <a href="/wiki/Physics" title="Physics">
           physics
          </a>
          and celestial mechanics. He kept up with the
          <a href="/wiki/New_Atlantis_Project" title="New Atlantis Project">
           Atlantis Project
          </a>
          on Earth through journals. Picard was fascinated to be the first to reveal an ancient
          <a href="/wiki/Promellian_battle_cruiser" title="Promellian battle cruiser">
           Promellian battle cruiser
          </a>
          , as visiting such an elegant craft was always a dream of Picard's, a dream he had held on to ever since he was a child when he used to build model ships in bottles. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Booby_Trap_(episode)" title="Booby Trap (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Booby Trap (TNG 3x06)">
            Booby Trap
           </span>
          </a>
          ") After his experience with the Kataan probe, Picard began to play the Ressikan flute and was good enough to perform works by
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mozart" title="Mozart">
           Mozart
          </a>
          . He considered the flute to be one of his most prized possessions. It represented, to him, an entire lifetime he lived in only 25 minutes. As of
          <a href="/wiki/2379" title="2379">
           2379
          </a>
          , Picard kept the flute on his desk in his
          <a href="/wiki/Captain%27s_ready_room" title="Captain's ready room">
           ready room
          </a>
          aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E. His attempts at
          <a href="/wiki/Painting" title="Painting">
           painting
          </a>
          were less successful. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Chase_(episode)" title="The Chase (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Chase (TNG 6x20)">
            The Chase
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Inner_Light_(episode)" title="The Inner Light (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Inner Light (TNG 5x25)">
            The Inner Light
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/A_Fistful_of_Datas_(episode)" title="A Fistful of Datas (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="A Fistful of Datas (TNG 6x08)">
            A Fistful of Datas
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/A_Matter_of_Perspective_(episode)" title="A Matter of Perspective (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="A Matter of Perspective (TNG 3x14)">
            A Matter of Perspective
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          Despite Picard being a rather private person, he maintained a good relationship with the members of his senior staff on board the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , but only joined in their weekly game of
          <a href="/wiki/Poker" title="Poker">
           poker
          </a>
          after seven years. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/All_Good_Things..._(episode)" title="All Good Things... (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="All Good Things... (TNG 7x25/26)">
            All Good Things...
           </span>
          </a>
          ") When enjoying the comforts of home on the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , Picard drank
          <a href="/wiki/Earl_Grey_tea" title="Earl Grey tea">
           Earl Grey tea
          </a>
          . He delighted in fencing, horseback riding, and his scale
          <a href="/wiki/Model" title="Model">
           models
          </a>
          of various
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet" title="Starfleet">
           Starfleet
          </a>
          vessels. His opponents in fencing included
          <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant" title="Lieutenant">
           Lieutenant
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Dean" title="Dean">
           Dean
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Guinan" title="Guinan">
           Guinan
          </a>
          , whom Picard coached in the sport. She initially lost one of their matches and said she did not think she liked the sport. Picard replied she liked it well enough two weeks prior, when she scored him two touches. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/We%27ll_Always_Have_Paris_(episode)" title="We'll Always Have Paris (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="We'll Always Have Paris (TNG 1x24)">
            We'll Always Have Paris
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/I_Borg_(episode)" title="I Borg (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="I Borg (TNG 5x23)">
            I Borg
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/3/3e/Picard_on_holiday.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070118203456&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard on holiday" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_on_holiday.jpg" data-image-name="Picard on holiday.jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/3/3e/Picard_on_holiday.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070118203456&amp;path-prefix=en" height="138" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard on holiday" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_on_holiday.jpg" data-image-name="Picard on holiday.jpg" height="138" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/3/3e/Picard_on_holiday.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070118203456&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_on_holiday.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard on holiday
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Only rarely did Picard take extended time off to relax. In
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , several of the members of his crew persuaded him to go on holiday on
          <a href="/wiki/Risa" title="Risa">
           Risa
          </a>
          . While intending to just relax in the suns, reading a book, he ended up going on a treasure hunt for the
          <a href="/wiki/Tox_Uthat" title="Tox Uthat">
           Tox Uthat
          </a>
          , an artifact from the future. (
