          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Captain%27s_Holiday_(episode)" title="Captain's Holiday (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Captain's Holiday (TNG 3x19)">
            Captain's Holiday
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Philosophically, Picard saw life and death as more than two choices of eternal or momentary existence. In fact, he believed there was another concept yet beyond
          <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">
           Human
          </a>
          understanding due to the marvelous complexity and the clockwork precision of the universe. In
          <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
           2364
          </a>
          , confronted by Q, Picard quoted from Shakespeare: "
          <i>
           What a piece of work is man? How noble in reason? How infinite in faculty, in form, in moving, how express and admirable. In action, how like an angel, in apprehension, how like a god...
          </i>
          " Upon Q's interruption that surely he did not see his own species like that, Picard answered that he saw Humankind one day becoming so. In Picard's opinion,
          <a href="/wiki/Genetic_engineering" title="Genetic engineering">
           genetic engineering
          </a>
          with its predetermination robbed Humanity of the unknown factor that makes life worth living. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Lonely_Among_Us_(episode)" title="Lonely Among Us (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Lonely Among Us (TNG 1x07)">
            Lonely Among Us
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Hide_and_Q_(episode)" title="Hide and Q (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Hide and Q (TNG 1x10)">
            Hide and Q
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Masterpiece_Society_(episode)" title="The Masterpiece Society (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Masterpiece Society (TNG 5x13)">
            The Masterpiece Society
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_relationships">
           Personal relationships
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit Personal relationships section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Family">
           Family
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit Family section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/b/b9/Troi_comforts_Picard.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100527075812&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Troi comforts Picard" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Troi_comforts_Picard.jpg" data-image-name="Troi comforts Picard.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/b/b9/Troi_comforts_Picard.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100527075812&amp;path-prefix=en" height="75" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Troi comforts Picard" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Troi_comforts_Picard.jpg" data-image-name="Troi comforts Picard.jpg" height="75" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/b/b9/Troi_comforts_Picard.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100527075812&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Troi_comforts_Picard.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard shows Deanna Troi his family photos
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Picard claimed that he was able to trace his family's roots in western
          <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">
           Europe
          </a>
          back to the time of
          <a href="/wiki/Charlemagne" title="Charlemagne">
           Charlemagne
          </a>
          in the
          <a href="/wiki/8th_century" title="8th century">
           8th century
          </a>
          . He had "never been a family man," and was thus long uncomfortable with the presence of children aboard the
          <a href="/wiki/Galaxy_class" title="Galaxy class">
           <i>
            Galaxy
           </i>
           -class
          </a>
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . The orphaned son of Lieutenant
          <a href="/wiki/Marla_Aster" title="Marla Aster">
           Marla Aster
          </a>
          again raised his concern about the vessel's civilian family contingent, although his unease with children had lessened since being stranded with three youths during a shipboard
          <a href="/wiki/Quantum_filament" title="Quantum filament">
           quantum filament
          </a>
          crisis. His time on Kataan also affected his views concerning family and children, as he admitted not being able to imagine a life without them. His initial reaction to family was also reflected in the friction with his father, and later his older brother, over leaving the family business. Upon the sudden accidental deaths of his brother
          <a href="/wiki/Robert_Picard" title="Robert Picard">
           Robert
          </a>
          and his nephew
          <a href="/wiki/Ren%C3%A9_Picard" title="Ren Picard">
           Ren
          </a>
          , the issue of lineage and Picard's lack of offspring caused a sustained yet brief period of depression. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Journey%27s_End_(episode)" title="Journey's End (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Journey's End (TNG 7x20)">
            Journey's End
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Bonding_(episode)" title="The Bonding (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Bonding (TNG 3x05)">
            The Bonding
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Disaster_(episode)" title="Disaster (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Disaster (TNG 5x05)">
            Disaster
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Inner_Light_(episode)" title="The Inner Light (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Inner Light (TNG 5x25)">
            The Inner Light
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Family_(episode)" title="Family (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Family (TNG 4x02)">
            Family
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Generations" title="Star Trek Generations">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Generations">
             Star Trek Generations
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2370" title="2370">
           2370
          </a>
          , DaiMon Bok threatened
          <a href="/wiki/Jason_Vigo" title="Jason Vigo">
           Jason Vigo
          </a>
          , claiming that Jason was Picard's son. It was soon revealed that Jason was not actually Picard's son. As a parting gift, Picard gave Jason an archaeological artifact of significant sentimental value. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Bloodlines_(episode)" title="Bloodlines (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Bloodlines (TNG 7x22)">
            Bloodlines
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Romance">
           Romance
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit Romance section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/19/Picard_and_Lwaxana_Troi.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121207032502&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard and Lwaxana Troi" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_and_Lwaxana_Troi.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Lwaxana Troi.jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/19/Picard_and_Lwaxana_Troi.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20121207032502&amp;path-prefix=en" height="134" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard and Lwaxana Troi" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_and_Lwaxana_Troi.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Lwaxana Troi.jpg" height="134" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/19/Picard_and_Lwaxana_Troi.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20121207032502&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_and_Lwaxana_Troi.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard and Ambassador Lwaxana Troi in 2365
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          When
          <a href="/wiki/Ambassador" title="Ambassador">
           Ambassador
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Lwaxana_Troi" title="Lwaxana Troi">
           Lwaxana Troi
          </a>
          visited the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-D)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-D)">
           USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -D
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/2365" title="2365">
           2365
          </a>
          , she had just entered her
          <a href="/wiki/Betazoid_phase" title="Betazoid phase">
           Betazoid phase
          </a>
          , and so she set her sights on several male crewmembers as potential mates, including Picard. She announced her "
          <a href="/wiki/Wedding" title="Wedding">
           wedding
          </a>
          " with William Riker on the
          <a href="/wiki/Bridge" title="Bridge">
           bridge
          </a>
          of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          shortly before moving on to Picard. Following an intimate dinner with the ambassador, Picard hid himself on the
          <a href="/wiki/Holodeck" title="Holodeck">
           holodeck
          </a>
          in a
          <a href="/wiki/Dixon_Hill_series" title="Dixon Hill series">
           Dixon Hill holonovel
          </a>
          . Lwaxana continued to teasingly flirt with Picard during her future visits to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . On one occasion, Picard pretended to be in love with Lwaxana in order to save the ambassador's daughter,
          <a href="/wiki/Deanna_Troi" title="Deanna Troi">
           Deanna Troi
          </a>
          , and Riker from Ferengi captivity. Lwaxana was most impressed with his Shakespearian poetry. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Manhunt_(episode)" title="Manhunt (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Manhunt (TNG 2x19)">
            Manhunt
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9nage_%C3%A0_Troi_(episode)" title="Mnage  Troi (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Mnage  Troi (TNG 3x24)">
            Mnage  Troi
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard had a relationship with an "adventurer" and some-time criminal named
          <a href="/wiki/Vash" title="Vash">
           Vash
          </a>
          . They initially met when Picard aided her attempts to find a rare artifact. Over the course of their adventure, the two developed an intimate relationship. Vash later returned to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          as part of an archaeological advisory team and was upset to find that Picard had not told his friends about their relationship. At the same time, Q appeared on the ship, and in return for Picard's aid in getting back to the Q Continuum, he created a
          <a href="/wiki/Robin_Hood" title="Robin Hood">
           Robin Hood
          </a>
          fantasy world in which Picard (Robin) had to save Vash (
          <a href="/wiki/Maid_Marian" title="Maid Marian">
           Maid Marian
          </a>
          ). Eventually, Vash and Picard parted on good terms, as she decided to travel the universe with Q. She later reappeared one last time on
          <a href="/wiki/Deep_Space_9" title="Deep Space 9">
           Deep Space 9
          </a>
          after being unceremoniously abandoned by her "partner" Q.
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2368" title="2368">
           2368
          </a>
          , while mediating negotiations between the warring planets
          <a href="/wiki/Krios" title="Krios">
           Krios
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Valt_Minor" title="Valt Minor">
           Valt Minor
          </a>
          , Picard encountered
          <a href="/wiki/Kamala" title="Kamala">
           Kamala
          </a>
          , an
          <a href="/wiki/Empathic_metamorph" title="Empathic metamorph">
           empathic metamorph
          </a>
          intended as a gift for
          <a href="/wiki/Valtese" title="Valtese">
           Valtese
          </a>
          Chancellor
          <a href="/wiki/Alrik" title="Alrik">
           Alrik
          </a>
          . Due to premature emergence from stasis, Kamala underwent her bonding phase before the marriage could be completed. When circumstances placed Picard and Kamala in close proximity to each other, she eventually bonded with the captain. However, having adapted to be perfectly compatible with Picard, Kamala found that her sense of duty demanded that she proceed with the marriage rather than pursue a relationship with Picard. Picard was deeply affected by Kamala, as shown by his reaction to Ambassador
          <a href="/wiki/Briam" title="Briam">
           Briam
          </a>
          's inquiry about the experience.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/ce/Picard_and_Daren_embrace.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140914220720&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard and Daren embrace" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_and_Daren_embrace.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Daren embrace.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/ce/Picard_and_Daren_embrace.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140914220720&amp;path-prefix=en" height="151" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard and Daren embrace" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_and_Daren_embrace.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Daren embrace.jpg" height="151" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/ce/Picard_and_Daren_embrace.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140914220720&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_and_Daren_embrace.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard and Nella Daren in 2369
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          , Lieutenant Commander
          <a href="/wiki/Nella_Daren" title="Nella Daren">
           Nella Daren
          </a>
          came aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          to become head of the ship's
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stellar_Cartography_department" title="Stellar Cartography department">
           Stellar Sciences department
          </a>
          . In her new role, she was very forthright in her requests for ship resources to support her department's studies. Soon after coming aboard, she and Picard met. A friendship quickly formed, based on their shared love for music. Daren accompanied the captain on a portable piano while he played the Ressikan flute. Their friendship soon blossomed into love. The crew reacted differently to Picard and Daren's romance: Deanna Troi was happy for Picard and gave her blessing; Beverly Crusher seemed jealous; and Riker felt that Daren was asking for special treatment because she was the captain's "girlfriend."
         </p>
         <p>
          When a fire storm threatened the
          <a href="/wiki/Bersallis_III" title="Bersallis III">
           Bersallis III
          </a>
          Federation
          <a href="/wiki/Outpost" title="Outpost">
           outpost
          </a>
          , Daren suggested a plan to shield the outpost against the heat while the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          evacuated the colonists. Eight crewmen lost their lives, but Daren survived. Afterward, it became obvious to Picard and Daren that it would be extremely difficult to continue their relationship while serving on the same ship, thus Daren requested a transfer. As they said goodbye, they promised to keep seeing each other, but knew their relationship would never be the same. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Lessons_(episode)" title="Lessons (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Lessons (TNG 6x19)">
            Lessons
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/9e/Anij_and_Picard_tour_the_village.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070623021619&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Anij and Picard tour the village" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Anij_and_Picard_tour_the_village.jpg" data-image-name="Anij and Picard tour the village.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/9e/Anij_and_Picard_tour_the_village.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070623021619&amp;path-prefix=en" height="76" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Anij and Picard tour the village" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Anij_and_Picard_tour_the_village.jpg" data-image-name="Anij and Picard tour the village.jpg" height="76" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/9/9e/Anij_and_Picard_tour_the_village.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070623021619&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Anij_and_Picard_tour_the_village.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard and Anij on Ba'ku
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2375" title="2375">
           2375
          </a>
          , Picard developed a short, though intimate relationship with the
          <a href="/wiki/Ba%27ku" title="Ba'ku">
           Ba'ku
          </a>
          woman
          <a href="/wiki/Anij" title="Anij">
           Anij
          </a>
          , while protecting her
          <a href="/wiki/Ba%27ku_(planet)" title="Ba'ku (planet)">
           homeworld
          </a>
          from the combined
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet" title="Starfleet">
           Starfleet
          </a>
          -
          <a href="/wiki/Son%27a" title="Son'a">
           Son'a
          </a>
          threat. Anij, while over 300 years old, appeared as a woman in her late 30s. Despite their intimacy, Picard returned to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          after the planned relocation of the Ba'ku was averted. Shortly before leaving, Picard said he had 318 days of vacation time coming, and that he planned on using them. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Insurrection" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
             Star Trek: Insurrection
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Beverly_Crusher">
           Beverly Crusher
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit Beverly Crusher section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/7/75/Jean-Luc_Picard_and_Beverly_Crusher_confide.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120921100509&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard and Beverly Crusher confide" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard_and_Beverly_Crusher_confide.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard and Beverly Crusher confide.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/7/75/Jean-Luc_Picard_and_Beverly_Crusher_confide.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120921100509&amp;path-prefix=en" height="139" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard and Beverly Crusher confide" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard_and_Beverly_Crusher_confide.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard and Beverly Crusher confide.jpg" height="139" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/7/75/Jean-Luc_Picard_and_Beverly_Crusher_confide.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120921100509&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean-Luc_Picard_and_Beverly_Crusher_confide.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard and Crusher in the captain's ready room
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          <a href="/wiki/Beverly_Crusher" title="Beverly Crusher">
           Beverly Crusher
          </a>
          and Picard maintained a close friendship while serving on the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -D, usually sharing their morning meal together. Crusher usually tried to serve a new and exotic food, although both she and Picard preferred something simple. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Attached_(episode)" title="Attached (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Attached (TNG 7x08)">
            Attached
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Their relationship stayed platonic, for the most part. They considered one another close friends and would give each other advice when dealing with difficult decisions. While Crusher was in anguish over
          <a href="/wiki/Odan" title="Odan">
           Odan
          </a>
          's failing health while the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Symbiont" title="Symbiont">
           symbiont
          </a>
          was in Riker's body, Picard gave her a hug, and assured her that he would always be her friend and be willing to help her any way he could. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Host_(episode)" title="The Host (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Host (TNG 4x23)">
            The Host
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Crusher's anger over the treatment of
          <a href="/wiki/Kamala" title="Kamala">
           Kamala
          </a>
          led to Picard spending time with her, where he quickly learned that he was falling for the metamorph. Crusher did not know what to say, but reciprocated the emotional support he had offered the year prior. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Perfect_Mate_(episode)" title="The Perfect Mate (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Perfect Mate (TNG 5x21)">
            The Perfect Mate
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard tried to make Crusher realize that the deaths of
          <a href="/wiki/Jo%27Bril" title="Jo'Bril">
           Jo'Bril
          </a>
          and later
          <a href="/wiki/Reyga" title="Reyga">
           Reyga
          </a>
          were not her fault and that she should not try to rush her investigation. Crusher was too upset and preoccupied to understand his words, and Picard was extremely disappointed when she broke the Prime Directive and performed an autopsy on Reyga. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Suspicions_(episode)" title="Suspicions (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Suspicions (TNG 6x22)">
            Suspicions
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard knew that Crusher's odd decisions after meeting
          <a href="/wiki/Ronin" title="Ronin">
           Ronin
          </a>
          were not normal and confronted her on
          <a href="/wiki/Caldos_colony" title="Caldos colony">
           Caldos colony
          </a>
          . Although Crusher initially resisted his demands for an explanation, she broke free of Ronin's influence after he attacked Picard. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Sub_Rosa_(episode)" title="Sub Rosa (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Sub Rosa (TNG 7x14)">
            Sub Rosa
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Early on, Crusher and Picard experienced several romantically close calls. Once she was under the influence of the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Psi_2000_intoxication" title="Psi 2000 intoxication">
           Psi 2000 intoxication
          </a>
          , Crusher flirted with Picard and attempted to seduce him on the bridge of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . Later, Crusher seemed hopeful for some time alone with Picard in the Dixon Hill holodeck simulation, but Picard seemed oblivious to her and invited Data and
          <a href="/wiki/Whalen" title="Whalen">
           Whalen
          </a>
          as well, much to Crusher's dismay. Commander
          <a href="/wiki/Dexter_Remmick" title="Dexter Remmick">
           Dexter Remmick
          </a>
          interrogated Crusher about Picard in mid-
          <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
           2364
          </a>
          and questioned her about her true feelings towards Picard. Crusher refused to answer, claiming that they were irrelevant to the operation of the ship. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Naked_Now_(episode)" title="The Naked Now (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Naked Now (TNG 1x03)">
            The Naked Now
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Big_Goodbye_(episode)" title="The Big Goodbye (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Big Goodbye (TNG 1x12)">
            The Big Goodbye
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Coming_of_Age_(episode)" title="Coming of Age (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Coming of Age (TNG 1x19)">
            Coming of Age
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , a
          <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard_(impostor)" title="Jean-Luc Picard (impostor)">
           duplicate of Picard
          </a>
          replaced the captain in order to learn about Human relationships. The impostor had all of the memories and experiences of Picard but his behavior was different from the captain. He was more outgoing and especially flirtatious with Dr. Crusher, inviting her to dinner, where the two had a romantic evening, including dancing. However, once the duplicate had enough information, it unceremoniously bade Crusher farewell. She teasingly held the real Picard responsible for his duplicate's actions when he was returned to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Allegiance_(episode)" title="Allegiance (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Allegiance (TNG 3x18)">
            Allegiance
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Several times, Crusher began to explain her true feelings to Picard, once while they were held captive on
          <a href="/wiki/Rutia_IV" title="Rutia IV">
           Rutia IV
          </a>
          , and another time with Picard's duplicate in the warp bubble universe, but she was interrupted in both instances. Both also displayed some jealousy when the other found a love interest, such as Crusher with Odan or Picard with
          <a href="/wiki/Jenice_Manheim" title="Jenice Manheim">
           Jenice Manheim
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Nella_Daren" title="Nella Daren">
           Nella Daren
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_High_Ground_(episode)" title="The High Ground (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The High Ground (TNG 3x12)">
            The High Ground
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Remember_Me_(episode)" title="Remember Me (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Remember Me (TNG 4x05)">
            Remember Me
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Host_(episode)" title="The Host (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Host (TNG 4x23)">
            The Host
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/We%27ll_Always_Have_Paris_(episode)" title="We'll Always Have Paris (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="We'll Always Have Paris (TNG 1x24)">
            We'll Always Have Paris
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Lessons_(episode)" title="Lessons (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Lessons (TNG 6x19)">
            Lessons
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/b/b6/Crusher_and_Picard_imprisoned.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141217024809&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Crusher and Picard imprisoned" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Crusher_and_Picard_imprisoned.jpg" data-image-name="Crusher and Picard imprisoned.jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/b/b6/Crusher_and_Picard_imprisoned.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141217024809&amp;path-prefix=en" height="135" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Crusher and Picard imprisoned" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Crusher_and_Picard_imprisoned.jpg" data-image-name="Crusher and Picard imprisoned.jpg" height="135" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/b/b6/Crusher_and_Picard_imprisoned.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141217024809&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Crusher_and_Picard_imprisoned.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Beverly and Picard telepathically attached on Kesprytt
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2370" title="2370">
           2370
          </a>
          , Picard and Crusher were taken captive on the planet
          <a href="/wiki/Kesprytt" title="Kesprytt">
           Kesprytt
          </a>
          , and linked together by
          <a href="/wiki/Psi-wave_device" title="Psi-wave device">
           psi-wave devices
          </a>
          in order to decrease their odds of escaping. The devices transmitted their thoughts to one another, where they learned each other's most intimate secrets. Crusher stayed up one night to listen to Picard's dreams, and Picard discovered that Crusher almost always had some biting comment at the ready, although she had learned to repress the urge to say them out loud. One night, Crusher brought up her late husband
          <a href="/wiki/Jack_Crusher" title="Jack Crusher">
           Jack
          </a>
          , and feelings of guilt washed over Picard. She finally learned that he, too, felt an attraction, but did not act on it out of respect for his dead friend. Once they returned to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , Picard expressed desire to further their relationship. However, Crusher ultimately decided that she did not want to ruin their friendship or be placed in a conflict of interest, and they decided to remain mutual friends. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Attached_(episode)" title="Attached (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Attached (TNG 7x08)">
            Attached
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In an
          <a href="/wiki/Anti-time_future" title="Anti-time future">
           unknown, alternate future timeframe
          </a>
          , Picard and Crusher were married, but had separated. Dr. Beverly Picard agreed to take Picard to the
          <a href="/wiki/Romulan_Neutral_Zone" title="Romulan Neutral Zone">
           Romulan Neutral Zone
          </a>
          aboard the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Pasteur" title="USS Pasteur">
           USS
           <i>
            Pasteur
           </i>
          </a>
          , an
          <a href="/wiki/Olympic_class" title="Olympic class">
           <i>
            Olympic
           </i>
           -class
          </a>
          medical vessel of which she was in command. They shared a kiss in the "present" during that time. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/All_Good_Things..._(episode)" title="All Good Things... (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="All Good Things... (TNG 7x25/26)">
            All Good Things...
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           The production staff kept Crusher and Picard from a serious romantic relationship to leave the captain free for possible movie story lines, such as that in
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Insurrection" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Insurrection">
            Star Trek: Insurrection
           </span>
          </a>
          <i>
           .
          </i>
          (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation_Companion" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation Companion">
            Star Trek: The Next Generation Companion
           </a>
          </i>
          )
          <i>
          </i>
         </div>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Friendships">
           Friendships
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit Friendships section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Guinan">
           Guinan
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit Guinan section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/68/Like_being_inside_joy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100527081430&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Like being inside joy" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Like_being_inside_joy.jpg" data-image-name="Like being inside joy.jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/68/Like_being_inside_joy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100527081430&amp;path-prefix=en" height="75" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Like being inside joy" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Like_being_inside_joy.jpg" data-image-name="Like being inside joy.jpg" height="75" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/6/68/Like_being_inside_joy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100527081430&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Like_being_inside_joy.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            With Guinan in her quarters in 2371
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Guinan and Picard shared a long-term relationship, which, according to her, went "beyond friendship and beyond family." (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds (TNG 3x26)">
            The Best of Both Worlds
           </span>
          </a>
          ") She also once said to Geordi La Forge that she was attracted to bald men. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Booby_Trap_(episode)" title="Booby Trap (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Booby Trap (TNG 3x06)">
            Booby Trap
           </span>
          </a>
          ") In return, Picard once observed Guinan to be "very selective about whom she calls a friend." (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Ensign_Ro_(episode)" title="Ensign Ro (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Ensign Ro (TNG 5x03)">
            Ensign Ro
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Guinan originally met Picard in
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1893" title="1893">
           1893
          </a>
          when he, Data, Riker, La Forge, Troi, and Dr. Crusher had traveled back in time from the
          <a href="/wiki/24th_century" title="24th century">
           24th century
          </a>
          to stop some
          <a href="/wiki/Devidian" title="Devidian">
           Devidians
          </a>
          from stealing energy from
          <a href="/wiki/Human" title="Human">
           Humans
          </a>
          in the
          <a href="/wiki/19th_century" title="19th century">
           19th century
          </a>
          . Guinan, learning of their predicament from Data who had thought she was the Guinan from the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-D)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-D)">
           USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -D
          </a>
          , agreed to help in any way she could. When she was injured in the confrontation with the Devidians, Picard stayed behind to make sure she was all right.
          <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Clemens" title="Samuel Clemens">
           Samuel Clemens
          </a>
          , returning from the 24th century, helped Picard return. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Time%27s_Arrow,_Part_II_(episode)" title="Time's Arrow, Part II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Time's Arrow, Part II (TNG 6x01)">
            Time's Arrow, Part II
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2365" title="2365">
           2365
          </a>
          , Data's rights as an individual were challenged when cybernetics expert Commander
          <a href="/wiki/Bruce_Maddox" title="Bruce Maddox">
           Bruce Maddox
          </a>
          wanted to disassemble the
          <a href="/wiki/Android" title="Android">
           android
          </a>
          for study. Picard challenged Maddox's assessment before the local
          <a href="/wiki/Judge_Advocate_General" title="Judge Advocate General">
           Judge Advocate General
          </a>
          . As the hearing neared its end, Picard admitted to Guinan he feared he was losing the case. Guinan asked what Maddox gained if he would be successful in disassembling and reassembling Data, and Picard responded he would possess the ability to build many more androids. He remembered Guinan's words that the decisions made today have implications for the future, and so Picard reasoned that if it would be decided that Data was indeed Starfleet property, all future androids would be also. Guinan noted there was an ancient word for that:
          <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">
           slavery
          </a>
          . Eventually, Picard won Data's case by pointing out that an entire race of Datas would be used as slaves, strictly against Federation principles. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Measure_Of_A_Man_(episode)" title="The Measure Of A Man (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Measure Of A Man (TNG 2x09)">
            The Measure Of A Man
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2367" title="2367">
           2367
          </a>
          , Guinan played the role of
          <a href="/wiki/Gloria" title="Gloria">
           Gloria
          </a>
          in one of Picard's Dixon Hill
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Holonovel" title="Holonovel">
           holonovels
          </a>
          . She, however, was not much impressed with the program. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Clues_(episode)" title="Clues (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Clues (TNG 4x14)">
            Clues
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Besides joining Picard on the holodeck, they would occasionally share a game of
          <a href="/wiki/Chess" title="Chess">
           chess
          </a>
          , and Guinan was also coached in
          <a href="/wiki/Fencing" title="Fencing">
           fencing
          </a>
          by Picard in
          <a href="/wiki/2368" title="2368">
           2368
          </a>
          , begun when she considered exercise to strengthen her arm. Shortly prior to their match, the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          had taken a Borg drone, later named
          <a href="/wiki/Hugh" title="Hugh">
           Hugh
          </a>
          , on board. Although Guinan initially questioned Picard's decision to have done so, she was convinced by La Forge to speak with the former drone. She could not, but acknowledged this Borg was developing a personality, becoming an individual. Upon her conversation with Hugh, she convinced Picard to speak with him as well. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/I_Borg_(episode)" title="I Borg (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="I Borg (TNG 5x23)">
            I Borg
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="William_T._Riker">
           William T. Riker
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit William T. Riker section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/cf/Worfpromotion.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100527075053&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Worfpromotion" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Worfpromotion.jpg" data-image-name="Worfpromotion.jpg" data-src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/cf/Worfpromotion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100527075053&amp;path-prefix=en" height="76" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Worfpromotion" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Worfpromotion.jpg" data-image-name="Worfpromotion.jpg" height="76" src="http://vignette1.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/c/cf/Worfpromotion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100527075053&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Worfpromotion.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard and Riker on the holodeck
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          When choosing a
          <a href="/wiki/First_officer" title="First officer">
           first officer
          </a>
          prior to the launch of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -D in 2363, Picard accessed the records of a number of candidates for the job. He eventually came across the record of one William T. Riker. Picard saw it as a glowing record filled with statistics that he felt told him nothing about the kind of officer Riker actually was. Picard was about to move on to the next candidate's record but stopped when he saw that a notation in Riker's record regarding an incident that took place on board the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Hood_(Excelsior_class)" title="USS Hood (Excelsior class)">
           USS
           <i>
            Hood
           </i>
          </a>
          in which Riker refused to allow Captain
          <a href="/wiki/Robert_DeSoto" title="Robert DeSoto">
           Robert DeSoto
          </a>
          to beam down to
          <a href="/wiki/Altair_III" title="Altair III">
           Altair III
          </a>
          . Picard was impressed that Riker would challenge his captain's authority if needed, and put the safety of the captain and the crew ahead of his own career if the need arose. This was a major factor in Picard's selection of Riker as his first officer  Picard wanted an officer who would not be afraid to stand up to him and be more concerned about the safety of the ship and mission than his personnel records. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Pegasus_(episode)" title="The Pegasus (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Pegasus (TNG 7x12)">
            The Pegasus
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard was very cold towards Riker during their first meeting and ordered the manual docking as a test of Riker's abilities. When he performed the docking with great expertise and skill, Picard formally greeted Riker, requesting that his new first officer make sure that he not allow Picard to "make an ass of himself" in front of the many children aboard the ship. One year later, Picard felt as if he had not done a good job of congratulating Riker, so he did it once more, this time making his feelings clear. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Encounter_at_Farpoint_(episode)" title="Encounter at Farpoint (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Encounter at Farpoint (TNG 1x01/02)">
            Encounter at Farpoint
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Icarus_Factor_(episode)" title="The Icarus Factor (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Icarus Factor (TNG 2x14)">
            The Icarus Factor
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Eventually, Riker and Picard became very good friends. With the best of intentions, Riker suggested that Picard vacation at Risa in
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , asking him to return with a
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Horga%27hn" title="Horga'hn">
            horga'hn
           </a>
          </i>
          . Picard did not realize the history behind the statue and kept it with him after purchasing it for Riker, making it appear as if the captain was seeking
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Jamaharon" title="Jamaharon">
            jamaharon
           </a>
          </i>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Captain%27s_Holiday_(episode)" title="Captain's Holiday (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Captain's Holiday (TNG 3x19)">
            Captain's Holiday
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          The only time Riker and Picard ever verbally fought in front of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          crew was in
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          while under the influence of emotions projected by Ambassador
          <a href="/wiki/Sarek" title="Sarek">
           Sarek
          </a>
          , who was suffering from
          <a href="/wiki/Bendii_Syndrome" title="Bendii Syndrome">
           Bendii Syndrome
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Sarek_(episode)" title="Sarek (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Sarek (TNG 3x23)">
            Sarek
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard tried to counsel Riker when he was offered command of the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Melbourne" title="USS Melbourne">
           USS
           <i>
            Melbourne
           </i>
          </a>
          in
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , reminding him that the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          would continue without his presence and that officers like
          <a href="/wiki/Shelby" title="Shelby">
           Shelby
          </a>
          were very much as he was before he learned the lessons necessary for command of a starship. Riker also came to Picard for advice when Worf wanted his help with the
          <i>
           hegh'bat
          </i>
          and when he struggled with a decision involving
          <a href="/wiki/Soren" title="Soren">
           Soren
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds (TNG 3x26)">
            The Best of Both Worlds
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Ethics_(episode)" title="Ethics (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Ethics (TNG 5x16)">
            Ethics
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Outcast_(episode)" title="The Outcast (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Outcast (TNG 5x17)">
            The Outcast
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/42/Number_One_Dad.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120518160803&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Number One Dad" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Number_One_Dad.jpg" data-image-name="Number One Dad.jpg" data-src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/42/Number_One_Dad.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120518160803&amp;path-prefix=en" height="168" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Number One Dad" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Number_One_Dad.jpg" data-image-name="Number One Dad.jpg" height="168" src="http://vignette2.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/4/42/Number_One_Dad.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120518160803&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Number_One_Dad.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            An age-reverted Picard pretends to be Riker's son
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In early
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          , members of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          crew, including Picard, were turned into twelve-year-olds due to the effects of a
          <a href="/wiki/Molecular_reversion_field" title="Molecular reversion field">
           molecular reversion field
          </a>
          . Unfortunately, a group of Ferengi commandeered the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          about that time. Believed to be a child, Picard was confined to a
          <a href="/wiki/Classroom" title="Classroom">
           classroom
          </a>
          aboard the ship while Riker was held in the
          <a href="/wiki/Observation_lounge" title="Observation lounge">
           observation lounge
          </a>
          . Picard threw a tantrum and demanded to see his "father," Riker. They pretended to be father and son in order for Picard to plant a suggestive message to Riker, requesting access to the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          main computer from the classroom. Picard, along with the other affected
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          crewmembers, were able to design a plan to retake the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          from the Ferengi. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Rascals_(episode)" title="Rascals (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Rascals (TNG 6x07)">
            Rascals
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          During the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Pegasus" title="USS Pegasus">
           <i>
            Pegasus
           </i>
          </a>
          incident of
          <a href="/wiki/2370" title="2370">
           2370
          </a>
          , Picard tried to investigate the circumstances surrounding the ship's disappearance. He ran into many dead-ends as most records had been sealed, and had to use many favors in
          <a href="/wiki/Starfleet_Command" title="Starfleet Command">
           Starfleet Command
          </a>
          to even get a look at the findings of the board convened to investigate the loss of the
          <i>
           Pegasus
          </i>
          . Riker would not divulge further information under the orders of Admiral
          <a href="/wiki/Erik_Pressman" title="Erik Pressman">
           Erik Pressman
          </a>
          , and Picard reluctantly continued the search. He made it clear to Riker that he hoped he still placed the safety of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          as his top priority, and if Picard had found this to be untrue, he would reevaluate his trust in Riker. After the crisis was resolved, Picard visited Riker in the
          <a href="/wiki/Brig" title="Brig">
           brig
          </a>
          and returned him to duty aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , understanding of Will's mistake in the past and satisfied that he had made the correct decisions in the present. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Pegasus_(episode)" title="The Pegasus (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Pegasus (TNG 7x12)">
            The Pegasus
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Picard served as Riker's best man during his
          <a href="/wiki/Wedding" title="Wedding">
           wedding
          </a>
          to Deanna Troi in
          <a href="/wiki/2379" title="2379">
           2379
          </a>
          . He gave a toast to Riker, calling him his "trusted right arm" and lamenting his loss of a fine first officer. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Data">
           Data
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit Data section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          From
          <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
           2364
          </a>
          to
          <a href="/wiki/2371" title="2371">
           2371
          </a>
          , Lieutenant Commander Data was appointed as
          <a href="/wiki/Operations_officer" title="Operations officer">
           head of operations
          </a>
          when serving on board the USS
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -D, and head of operations from
          <a href="/wiki/2372" title="2372">
           2372
          </a>
          to
          <a href="/wiki/2379" title="2379">
           2379
          </a>
          on board the USS
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E. Data looked up to Picard as something of a father figure throughout his service under the captain, asking for his advice on numerous occasions in his quest to become more Human. Picard always gave Data advice whenever he could.
         </p>
         <p>
          Following Natasha Yar's death in
          <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
           2364
          </a>
          , Data was puzzled about her death, thinking not about Tasha but rather how he would feel in her absence, thinking that he missed the purpose of her memorial, but Picard assured him that he understood the purpose of the memorial perfectly. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Skin_of_Evil_(episode)" title="Skin of Evil (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Skin of Evil (TNG 1x23)">
            Skin of Evil
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/a/ae/Picard_defends_Data.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121210232026&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard defends Data" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_defends_Data.jpg" data-image-name="Picard defends Data.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/a/ae/Picard_defends_Data.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20121210232026&amp;path-prefix=en" height="134" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard defends Data" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_defends_Data.jpg" data-image-name="Picard defends Data.jpg" height="134" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/a/ae/Picard_defends_Data.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20121210232026&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_defends_Data.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard defends Data's rights as an individual
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2365" title="2365">
           2365
          </a>
          , Data's existence was threatened when Commander Bruce Maddox wished to disassemble and study Data to gain a better understanding of how his
          <a href="/wiki/Positronic_brain" title="Positronic brain">
           positronic brain
          </a>
          functioned. Data refused to submit to Maddox's procedure, finding his research flawed, but Maddox claimed that Data was property of Starfleet and therefore not a sentient being and as a result had no choice other than to submit to the procedure. Captain Phillipa Louvois supported Maddox's claim, and Picard intervened by challenging their reasoning, saying that Data was indeed sentient and deserved the freedom to make his own decisions. He also said that Data represented an entire race and that forcing him to submit to Maddox's procedure is tantamount to slavery  strictly against Federation law. Ultimately, Louvois sided with Picard's standpoint and agreed that Data, android or not, was indeed sentient and entitled to the same rights as any other Starfleet officer. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Measure_Of_A_Man_(episode)" title="The Measure Of A Man (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Measure Of A Man (TNG 2x09)">
            The Measure Of A Man
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2367" title="2367">
           2367
          </a>
          , Picard's seemingly unbreakable trust in Data was tested when Data refused to fully cooperate with an investigation into a number of events that happened within a 24-hour time span, although Data claimed that the time span was only 30 seconds. Data's intransigence threatened to end his Starfleet career and even his own existence, but it was later revealed that Picard was himself responsible for Data's unusual behavior after an encounter with the
          <a href="/wiki/Paxan" title="Paxan">
           Paxans
          </a>
          in a
          <a href="/wiki/T-Tauri_type" title="T-Tauri type">
           T-Tauri type
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_system" title="Star system">
           star system
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Clues_(episode)" title="Clues (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Clues (TNG 4x14)">
            Clues
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          During the
          <a href="/wiki/Klingon_Civil_War" title="Klingon Civil War">
           Klingon Civil War
          </a>
          , the Federation made an indirect intervention with a blockade of Starfleet vessels placed in formation to use the pioneering
          <a href="/wiki/Tachyon_detection_grid" title="Tachyon detection grid">
           tachyon detection grid
          </a>
          in an effort to expose Romulan support for the
          <a href="/wiki/House_of_Duras" title="House of Duras">
           House of Duras
          </a>
          . Picard assigned all of his senior officers positions on board other ships, except for Data. Data questioned Picard about why he was not assigned command of a vessel, considering that there was a severe lack of senior officers available for the mission, wondering if he felt that his being an android made him unsuitable for command. Picard, slightly embarrassed by Data's question, assigned Data command of the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Sutherland" title="USS Sutherland">
           USS
           <i>
            Sutherland
           </i>
          </a>
          . During the blockade, Data disobeyed direct orders from Picard and was able to expose the Romulans' involvement in the civil war. Later, Data wished to submit himself for disciplinary action for disobeying a direct order from his superior officer, but Picard instead praised Data for
          <i>
           not
          </i>
          complying, summing up his belief of too many tragedies throughout history being directly traceable to officers "just following orders" rather than independently assessing their situations, with the words, "
          <i>
           Mr. Data: nicely done.
          </i>
          " (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_II_(episode)" title="Redemption II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption II (TNG 5x01)">
            Redemption II
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          , Data refused to allow a group of
          <a href="/wiki/Exocomp" title="Exocomp">
           exocomps
          </a>
          to be sacrificed in order to save the lives of Picard and Geordi La Forge, who were trapped on board the
          <a href="/wiki/Particle_Fountain_Project" title="Particle Fountain Project">
           Particle Fountain Project
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Space_station" title="Space station">
           space station
          </a>
          , believing that they were sentient and, therefore, capable of making their own decisions. After agreeing to a compromise suggested by Commander William Riker, the exocomps were released and able to save the lives of Picard and La Forge. Picard understood the predicament that Data was faced with as he had defended Data's sentience just a few years previously, but this time the exocomps had no advocate and Data felt compelled to act on their behalf. Picard considered Data's actions to be the most "Human" decision that he had ever made. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Quality_of_Life_(episode)" title="The Quality of Life (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Quality of Life (TNG 6x09)">
            The Quality of Life
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Later that year, following an accident in
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Main_engineering" title="Main engineering">
           main engineering
          </a>
          that activated a dormant program in his positronic brain, Data sought advice from several officers, including Picard, on his "visions." Picard was curious why Data was studying thousands of different cultures to
          <a href="/wiki/Metaphysics" title="Metaphysics">
           interpret
          </a>
          his visions. Data said that he had no culture of his own, but Picard told Data that he did have a culture  a culture of one and that its validity is no less than that of a billion. Picard suggested that Data should consider what the visions meant to him instead of what they mean to other people. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Birthright,_Part_I_(episode)" title="Birthright, Part I (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Birthright, Part I (TNG 6x16)">
            Birthright, Part I
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          After a malfunctioning
          <a href="/wiki/Emotion_chip" title="Emotion chip">
           emotion chip
          </a>
          fused with Data's positronic net in
          <a href="/wiki/2371" title="2371">
           2371
          </a>
          , Data felt guilty for not saving La Forge from capture by
          <a href="/wiki/Tolian_Soran" title="Tolian Soran">
           Tolian Soran
          </a>
          on board the
          <a href="/wiki/Amargosa_observatory" title="Amargosa observatory">
           Amargosa observatory
          </a>
          . Overwhelmed by emotions, Data requested to be shut down until the chip could be removed. Although Picard felt sympathy for Data, he told him that part of having emotions is integrating them into one's life and learning to live with them, and denied Data his request. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Generations" title="Star Trek Generations">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Generations">
             Star Trek Generations
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
