          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/d/dc/Picard_and_Data_hunt_Borg.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120318011444&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard and Data hunt Borg" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_and_Data_hunt_Borg.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Data hunt Borg.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/d/dc/Picard_and_Data_hunt_Borg.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120318011444&amp;path-prefix=en" height="77" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard and Data hunt Borg" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_and_Data_hunt_Borg.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Data hunt Borg.jpg" height="77" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/d/dc/Picard_and_Data_hunt_Borg.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120318011444&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_and_Data_hunt_Borg.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard and Data defend the
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
            -E from a Borg invasion
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2373" title="2373">
           2373
          </a>
          , when the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E traveled back to the year
          <a href="/wiki/2063" title="2063">
           2063
          </a>
          on Earth, Picard and Data initially went down to the planet to observe the damage the Borg had done to
          <a href="/wiki/Zefram_Cochrane" title="Zefram Cochrane">
           Zefram Cochrane
          </a>
          's missile complex in
          <a href="/wiki/Montana" title="Montana">
           Montana
          </a>
          . Down in the missile silo of the
          <i>
           Phoenix
          </i>
          , Picard, upon touching the missile that would make history by becoming the first Human starship traveling at
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Warp" title="Warp">
           warp
          </a>
          , explained to Data that sometimes a touch can make objects more "real." Upon suspecting a Borg presence aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , Picard and Data transported back to the ship. Fighting off the Borg near main engineering, Data was soon captured and brought to the Borg Queen. Instead of attempting to
          <a href="/wiki/Assimilation" title="Assimilation">
           assimilate
          </a>
          Data, the Queen made him physically more Human by attaching Human skin onto his android skeleton.
         </p>
         <p>
          When it appeared impossible to hold off the Borg any longer, Picard was convinced to initiate the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          's
          <a href="/wiki/Auto-destruct" title="Auto-destruct">
           auto-destruct
          </a>
          sequence and ordered all remaining crew to evacuate. He himself went on to engineering to find Data and to convince the Queen, who he had encountered several years previously, to let Data go. Picard was even prepared to take Data's place at the Queen's side, willingly becoming her equal. Data, however, claimed he did not wish to go, even after the Queen ordered him away. Thus, the Queen ordered Picard's assimilation, but not before witnessing the destruction of the
          <i>
           Phoenix
          </i>
          by Data.
         </p>
         <p>
          Data fired a spread of
          <a href="/wiki/Quantum_torpedo" title="Quantum torpedo">
           quantum torpedoes
          </a>
          , but they missed by the smallest of margins. Quickly thereafter, he burst a
          <a href="/wiki/Plasma_coolant" title="Plasma coolant">
           plasma coolant
          </a>
          tank, releasing plasma coolant which liquefied organic material on contact, killing the Borg. The Queen was killed, but Picard survived. Helping Data standing up, Picard asked him if he was ever tempted to join the Borg's cause. Data replied that, for a fraction of a second, hinting at his kiss with the Queen, he was. He added that, for an android, that brief moment was like an eternity. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/12/Picard_and_Data_%282379%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20050609092256&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard and Data (2379)" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard_and_Data_%282379%29.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Data (2379).jpg" data-src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/12/Picard_and_Data_%282379%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20050609092256&amp;path-prefix=en" height="83" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard and Data (2379)" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard_and_Data_%282379%29.jpg" data-image-name="Picard and Data (2379).jpg" height="83" src="http://vignette4.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/12/Picard_and_Data_%282379%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20050609092256&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard_and_Data_(2379).jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Data sacrifices himself to save Picard aboard the Reman vessel
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Following the wedding of Riker and Deanna Troi in
          <a href="/wiki/2379" title="2379">
           2379
          </a>
          , Data was confused by Picard's mixed feelings for the couple  although the captain was happy that Will was due to accept promotion to the rank of captain and take command of the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Titan" title="USS Titan">
           USS
           <i>
            Titan
           </i>
          </a>
          , and that his new wife was to transfer over to the
          <i>
           Titan
          </i>
          and take position as the ship's
          <a href="/wiki/Counselor" title="Counselor">
           counselor
          </a>
          , Picard was somewhat saddened by their departure and tried to explain to Data that experiencing feelings of both happiness and sadness at the same time are common in these situations.
         </p>
         <p>
          At the climax of the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Bassen_Rift" title="Battle of the Bassen Rift">
           Battle of the Bassen Rift
          </a>
          , Data jumped across the void of space from the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E to the
          <i>
           Scimitar
          </i>
          , saving Picard by using a prototype
          <a href="/wiki/Emergency_transport_unit" title="Emergency transport unit">
           emergency transport unit
          </a>
          , but sacrificed his own life to save the crew of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          by firing at the thalaron radiation generator and so destroying the
          <i>
           Scimitar
          </i>
          . Following the battle, Picard held a toast with the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E's senior officers as a tribute to their fallen comrade. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Worf">
           Worf
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit Worf section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          By
          <a href="/wiki/2364" title="2364">
           2364
          </a>
          , Lieutenant junior grade Worf was serving on the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -D as a junior bridge officer under Picard's command. Upon the death of Lieutenant Natasha Yar, he was promoted to
          <a href="/wiki/Chief_tactical_officer" title="Chief tactical officer">
           chief tactical officer
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Security_chief" title="Security chief">
           security chief
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Encounter_at_Farpoint_(episode)" title="Encounter at Farpoint (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Encounter at Farpoint (TNG 1x01/02)">
            Encounter at Farpoint
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Skin_of_Evil_(episode)" title="Skin of Evil (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Skin of Evil (TNG 1x23)">
            Skin of Evil
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Child_(episode)" title="The Child (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Child (TNG 2x01)">
            The Child
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
           2366
          </a>
          , the
          <a href="/wiki/Klingon_High_Council" title="Klingon High Council">
           Klingon High Council
          </a>
          accused
          <a href="/wiki/Mogh" title="Mogh">
           Mogh
          </a>
          , the deceased father of Lieutenant Worf, of treason. Picard, understanding the severity of the charges and their implications for Worf, had the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          change course to
          <a href="/wiki/Qo%27noS" title="Qo'noS">
           Qo'noS
          </a>
          .  Worf's brother
          <a href="/wiki/Kurn" title="Kurn">
           Kurn
          </a>
          initially served as his
          <a href="/wiki/Cha%27DIch" title="Cha'DIch">
           Cha'DIch
          </a>
          , but after an assassination attempt left him in critical condition, Worf asked Picard to take up the role.  Picard initially declined, saying that there were younger, more able men on the ship from which Worf could choose. However, Worf insisted that there was no one he would rather have at his side. Picard accepted and stood by Worf when the conspiracy against his family was uncovered. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Sins_of_the_Father_(episode)" title="Sins of the Father (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Sins of the Father (TNG 3x17)">
            Sins of the Father
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          When the Klingon Civil War erupted in
          <a href="/wiki/2367" title="2367">
           2367
          </a>
          , Worf resigned from Starfleet and fought on the side of
          <a href="/wiki/Gowron" title="Gowron">
           Gowron
          </a>
          against the forces of the
          <a href="/wiki/House_of_Duras" title="House of Duras">
           Duras
          </a>
          family. With the help of Picard, Worf and other Gowron supporters revealed
          <a href="/wiki/Romulan" title="Romulan">
           Romulan
          </a>
          assistance to the Duras cause. This collapsed support for the House of Duras, and Gowron won the chancellorship. Gowron restored the honor of the
          <a href="/wiki/House_of_Mogh" title="House of Mogh">
           House of Mogh
          </a>
          in thanks for its assistance during the war. Worf returned to Starfleet, but was reprimanded because he killed Duras in revenge. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_(episode)" title="Redemption (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption (TNG 4x26)">
            Redemption
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_II_(episode)" title="Redemption II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption II (TNG 5x01)">
            Redemption II
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <figure class="article-thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/16/WorfpicardFC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101119174454&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="WorfpicardFC" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="WorfpicardFC.jpg" data-image-name="WorfpicardFC.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/16/WorfpicardFC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101119174454&amp;path-prefix=en" height="77" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="WorfpicardFC" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="WorfpicardFC.jpg" data-image-name="WorfpicardFC.jpg" height="77" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/16/WorfpicardFC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101119174454&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:WorfpicardFC.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Worf and Picard shake hands aboard the
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
            -E
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Worf commanded the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Defiant_(2370)" title="USS Defiant (2370)">
           USS
           <i>
            Defiant
           </i>
          </a>
          in the battle against the Borg at
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Sector_001" title="Battle of Sector 001">
           Sector 001
          </a>
          , and fought the Borg temporal incursion into
          <a href="/wiki/2063" title="2063">
           2063
          </a>
          . A heated conflict occurred between the two when Picard had called Worf a "coward" for not wanting to continue fighting the Borg aboard the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -E, and a furious Worf stating that if he were any other man he would kill him where he stood, to which Picard angrily ordered Worf off his bridge. Picard later apologized to Worf for his harsh comments and admitted that Worf was "the bravest man" he had ever known, and their friendship was restored. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Geordi_La_Forge">
           Geordi La Forge
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit Geordi La Forge section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          Like several crew members,
          <a href="/wiki/Geordi_La_Forge" title="Geordi La Forge">
           Geordi La Forge
          </a>
          was hand picked by Picard to serve aboard the Enterprise-D. Geordi impressed Picard with his above average work ethic during an inspection tour. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Next_Phase_(episode)" title="The Next Phase (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Next Phase (TNG 5x24)">
            The Next Phase
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Picard has tremendous confidence in La Forge's ability to accomplish tasks he is assigned, which led to his eventual promotion to Chief Engineer, earning him the rank of Lieutenant Commander. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Child_(episode)" title="The Child (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Child (TNG 2x01)">
            The Child
           </span>
          </a>
          ") He is one of the very few officers Picard addresses by his first name, indicating a close bond between them.
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Ro_Laren">
           Ro Laren
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit Ro Laren section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          Picard and Laren had what could be described as a father/daughter-like relationship. When they first met, Picard wrote her off as dishonorable. He did, however, eventually take her under his wing and help her along a path towards redemption. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Ensign_Ro_(episode)" title="Ensign Ro (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Ensign Ro (TNG 5x03)">
            Ensign Ro
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Upon Ro's defection to a terrorist organization, she asked Will Riker to convey her deepest regrets to Picard for letting him down. Despite this, Picard was severely disillusioned by Ro's actions and felt betrayed in a very personal way. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Preemptive_Strike_(episode)" title="Preemptive Strike (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Preemptive Strike (TNG 7x24)">
            Preemptive Strike
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">
           Allies
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit Allies section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="James_T._Kirk">
           James T. Kirk
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit James T. Kirk section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          Although their association was brief,
          <a href="/wiki/James_T._Kirk" title="James T. Kirk">
           James T. Kirk
          </a>
          and Jean-Luc Picard had profound personal effects on one another. Very much like Spock and Leonard McCoy, Picard was instrumental in helping Kirk find meaning in his life after his greatest adventures were essentially over. In fact it could be argued that Picard is one of the most significant persons in Kirk's entire life, as he embarked on his final adventure with him and passed away knowing that he had "made a difference." Picard laid Kirk to rest on that obscure planet and was his lone mourner. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Generations" title="Star Trek Generations">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Generations">
             Star Trek Generations
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Spock">
           Spock
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit Spock section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          <a href="/wiki/Spock" title="Spock">
           Spock
          </a>
          was confronted by Picard and Data on
          <a href="/wiki/Romulus" title="Romulus">
           Romulus
          </a>
          , where he was suspected to have betrayed the Federation. To the contrary, Spock was on a "personal mission of peace," and Picard insisted on staying until Spock's affairs were complete. Spock saw much of his father,
          <a href="/wiki/Sarek" title="Sarek">
           Sarek
          </a>
          , in Picard and was very resentful of his perceived meddling in his affairs. However, Picard and Spock eventually developed a mutual respect for each other, with Picard offering Spock to
          <a href="/wiki/Vulcan_mind_meld" title="Vulcan mind meld">
           mind meld
          </a>
          with him to see how Sarek truly saw his son. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Unification_I_(episode)" title="Unification I (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Unification I (TNG 5x07)">
            Unification I
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Unification_II_(episode)" title="Unification II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Unification II (TNG 5x08)">
            Unification II
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Spock would later utilize Picard and
          <a href="/wiki/Deanna_Troi" title="Deanna Troi">
           Deanna Troi
          </a>
          in delivering defecting Romulan officials to the Federation. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Face_of_the_Enemy_(episode)" title="Face of the Enemy (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Face of the Enemy (TNG 6x14)">
            Face of the Enemy
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           Picard stated in the episode "
           <a href="/wiki/Sarek_(episode)" title="Sarek (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Sarek (TNG 3x23)">
             Sarek
            </span>
           </a>
           " that, as a lieutenant, he had briefly met with Sarek at the wedding of the latter's son. Episode writer
           <a href="/wiki/Ira_Steven_Behr" title="Ira Steven Behr">
            Ira Steven Behr
           </a>
           recalled that caution was still in place during early
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           The Next Generation
          </a>
          <i>
           about dealing with characters from
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Original_Series" title="Star Trek: The Original Series">
           The Original Series
          </a>
          <i>
           , thus it was only implied that the son in question was Spock. (
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation_Companion" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation Companion">
           Star Trek: The Next Generation Companion
          </a>
          <i>
           )
           <div style="margin-top:.5em">
            If it was indeed Spock's wedding, it would have occurred between 2327 and 2333. Since Picard graduated from Starfleet Academy in 2327 and was promoted to lieutenant commander when he was given command of the
            <a href="/wiki/USS_Stargazer" title="USS Stargazer">
             USS
             <i>
              Stargazer
             </i>
            </a>
            in 2333, he was a lieutenant at some point during the intervening time span.
           </div>
           <div style="margin-top:.5em">
            In the novel
            <a href="/wiki/Vulcan%27s_Heart" title="Vulcan's Heart">
             Vulcan's Heart
            </a>
            <i>
             , it is the wedding of Spock and Saavik, in 2329, and Lt. Picard, not really knowing why he was there, spends most of it in the company of one of the few other Humans in attendance, Leonard McCoy.
            </i>
           </div>
          </i>
         </div>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Gowron">
           Gowron
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit Gowron section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          Picard was
          <a href="/wiki/Gowron" title="Gowron">
           Gowron
          </a>
          's Arbiter of Succession following the deaths of
          <a href="/wiki/K%27mpec" title="K'mpec">
           K'mpec
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Duras,_son_of_Ja%27rod" title="Duras, son of Ja'rod">
           Duras
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Reunion_(episode)" title="Reunion (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Reunion (TNG 4x07)">
            Reunion
           </span>
          </a>
          ") Although he initially refused to aid him during the Klingon Civil War, Picard later convinced Starfleet to assist Gowron's forces by exposing the alliance between
          <a href="/wiki/Lursa" title="Lursa">
           Lursa
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/B%27Etor" title="B'Etor">
           B'Etor
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/Sela" title="Sela">
           Sela
          </a>
          , a high-ranking Romulan officer. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_(episode)" title="Redemption (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption (TNG 4x26)">
            Redemption
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_II_(episode)" title="Redemption II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption II (TNG 5x01)">
            Redemption II
           </span>
          </a>
          "). Although he considered Picard an honorable ally of the Klingon Empire, Gowron was less than accommodating when asked to assist Starfleet find
          <a href="/wiki/Spock" title="Spock">
           Spock
          </a>
          on Romulus. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Unification_I_(episode)" title="Unification I (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Unification I (TNG 5x07)">
            Unification I
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Unification_II_(episode)" title="Unification II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Unification II (TNG 5x08)">
            Unification II
           </span>
          </a>
          ") However, these events appeared to be reconciled during the events surrounding the resurrection of
          <a href="/wiki/Kahless_(clone)" title="Kahless (clone)">
           Kahless
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Rightful_Heir_(episode)" title="Rightful Heir (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Rightful Heir (TNG 6x23)">
            Rightful Heir
           </span>
          </a>
          ") It is unknown how Picard reacted when learning of Gowron's withdrawal from the
          <a href="/wiki/Khitomer_Accords" title="Khitomer Accords">
           Khitomer Accords
          </a>
          during the run up to the
          <a href="/wiki/Klingon-Cardassian_War" title="Klingon-Cardassian War">
           Klingon-Cardassian War
          </a>
          (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
            DS9
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Way_of_the_Warrior_(episode)" title="The Way of the Warrior (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Way of the Warrior (DS9 4x01/02)">
            The Way of the Warrior
           </span>
          </a>
          ") or his death at the hands of
          <a href="/wiki/Worf" title="Worf">
           Worf
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
            DS9
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Tacking_Into_the_Wind_(episode)" title="Tacking Into the Wind (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tacking Into the Wind (DS9 7x22)">
            Tacking Into the Wind
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Rivals">
           Rivals
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit Rivals section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Q">
           Q
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit Q section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          <a href="/wiki/Q" title="Q">
           Q
          </a>
          and Picard had a complicated relationship. Even though he was very antagonistic towards them, Q clearly had a great respect and affection for the crew of the Enterprise-D, particularly Picard (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Qpid_(episode)" title="Qpid (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Qpid (TNG 4x20)">
            Qpid
           </span>
          </a>
          "), who in contrast views Q with a tremendous amount of disdain and distrust (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Deja_Q_(episode)" title="Deja Q (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Deja Q (TNG 3x13)">
            Deja Q
           </span>
          </a>
          "). It was not until their final two known encounters that Picard became grateful to Q for their association. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
            Tapestry
           </span>
          </a>
          "), (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/All_Good_Things..._(episode)" title="All Good Things... (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="All Good Things... (TNG 7x25/26)">
            All Good Things...
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Shinzon">
           Shinzon
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit Shinzon section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          As a direct clone of Picard,
          <a href="/wiki/Shinzon" title="Shinzon">
           Shinzon
          </a>
          's developed a distinctive and deadly rivalry with the captain of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          , much like Will Riker's rivalry with
          <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Riker" title="Thomas Riker">
           Thomas Riker
          </a>
          and Data's rivalry with
          <a href="/wiki/Lore" title="Lore">
           Lore
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Second_Chances_(episode)" title="Second Chances (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Second Chances (TNG 6x24)">
            Second Chances
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Brothers_(episode)" title="Brothers (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Brothers (TNG 4x03)">
            Brothers
           </span>
          </a>
          ")  Picard saw traits in Shinzon that he perceived to be flaws within himself. He was bothered by the fact that Shinzon was capable of genocides of interstellar magnitude and was haunted by the notion that he may have chosen the same path as Shinzon had he led his life. During Shinzon's attempt to carry out these genocides, Picard implored him to let go of his past and embrace change, which Shinzon quickly rejected. Picard was significantly pained at the death of Shinzon, but this pain was replaced mere moments later after Data sacrificed himself to save Picard. (
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Nemesis" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Nemesis">
             Star Trek Nemesis
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="The_House_of_Duras">
           The House of Duras
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit The House of Duras section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          Jean-Luc Picard became a prominent figure in Klingon politics, largely due to his loyalty to Worf during the trial of the
          <a href="/wiki/House_of_Mogh" title="House of Mogh">
           House of Mogh
          </a>
          in 2366. Picard was determined to uncover the conspiracy that was attempting to frame
          <a href="/wiki/Mogh" title="Mogh">
           Mogh
          </a>
          for crimes committed by
          <a href="/wiki/Ja%27rod" title="Ja'rod">
           Ja'rod
          </a>
          . During his investigation,
          <a href="/wiki/Duras,_son_of_Ja%27rod" title="Duras, son of Ja'rod">
           Duras, son of Ja'rod
          </a>
          sent an assassin to murder Picard, but the attempt was unsuccessful and ultimately revealed the complicity of
          <a href="/wiki/K%27mpec" title="K'mpec">
           K'mpec
          </a>
          and the High Council in these crimes. Even after the death of Duras at the hands of Worf, the
          <a href="/wiki/House_of_Duras" title="House of Duras">
           House of Duras
          </a>
          continued to be antagonistic towards the Federation, with particular emphasis placed on Picard and the crew of the
          <i>
           Enterprise
          </i>
          -D, which was eventually destroyed by
          <a href="/wiki/Lursa" title="Lursa">
           Lursa
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/B%27Etor" title="B'Etor">
           B'Etor
          </a>
          . (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Sins_of_the_Father_(episode)" title="Sins of the Father (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Sins of the Father (TNG 3x17)">
            Sins of the Father
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_(episode)" title="Redemption (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption (TNG 4x26)">
            Redemption
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Redemption_II_(episode)" title="Redemption II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Redemption II (TNG 5x01)">
            Redemption II
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Generations" title="Star Trek Generations">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Generations">
             Star Trek Generations
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Bok">
           Bok
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit Bok section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          After the death of his son caused by Captain Picard during the
          <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Maxia" title="Battle of Maxia">
           Battle of Maxia
          </a>
          , Bok had tried to seek vengeance on him twice. First by having him destroy the
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Enterprise-D" title="Enterprise-D">
           Enterprise-D
          </a>
          through a mind altering device he hid within the derelict of the
          <a href="/wiki/USS_Stargazer" title="USS Stargazer">
           USS Stargazer
          </a>
          , then by attempting to kill his alleged son
          <a href="/wiki/Jason_Vigo" title="Jason Vigo">
           Jason Vigo
          </a>
          (which whom he re-sequenced his DNA in order to fool Picard into thinking he was his son). (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Battle_(episode)" title="The Battle (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Battle (TNG 1x09)">
            The Battle
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Bloodlines_(episode)" title="Bloodlines (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Bloodlines (TNG 7x22)">
            Bloodlines
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          <br/>
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="The_Borg.2FBorg_Queen">
           The Borg/Borg Queen
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit The Borg/Borg Queen section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          After being assimilated by The Borg, Picard (assuming the identity of Locutus) then went to destroy nearly all Federation Starships at the Battle of Wolf 359 before proceeding to Earth for an attempted assimilation of that Planet.After being de-assimilated, Picard had long resented the fact that The Borg had used his knowledge and experience to kill and/or assimilate innocent people. Almost to the point where he had enjoyed killing drones. This resentment had stayed with him at least six years after he was first assimilated. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            TNG
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds (TNG 3x26)">
            The Best of Both Worlds
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds,_Part_II_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (TNG 4x01)">
            The Best of Both Worlds, Part II
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Reunion_(episode)" title="Reunion (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Reunion (TNG 4x07)">
            Reunion
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/I_Borg_(episode)" title="I Borg (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="I Borg (TNG 5x23)">
            I Borg
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Descent_(episode)" title="Descent (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Descent (TNG 6x26)">
            Descent
           </span>
          </a>
          ", "
          <a href="/wiki/Descent,_Part_II_(episode)" title="Descent, Part II (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Descent, Part II (TNG 7x01)">
            Descent, Part II
           </span>
          </a>
          ";
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_First_Contact" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: First Contact">
             Star Trek: First Contact
            </span>
           </a>
          </i>
          )
         </p>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Alternate_realities_and_timelines">
           Alternate realities and timelines
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit Alternate realities and timelines section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <ul>
          <li>
           In
           <a href="/wiki/2365" title="2365">
            2365
           </a>
           , the
           <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-D)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-D)">
            USS
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
            -D
           </a>
           was pulled into an
           <a href="/wiki/Energy_vortex" title="Energy vortex">
            energy vortex
           </a>
           and could not return to normal space. In order not to be pulled even further, La Forge had to hold the ship at maximum warp, but such power drainage threatened to destroy the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           . Thinking that the vortex recognized him as the "brain" of the ship and wanted him, and not the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           , Picard boarded the
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shuttle" title="Shuttle">
            shuttle
           </a>
           <a href="/wiki/El-Baz" title="El-Baz">
            El-Baz
           </a>
           and left the vessel. The
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           was still destroyed, and the
           <i>
            El-Baz
           </i>
           was pulled six hours back in time, where it was picked up by that time period's
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           . Picard encountered his past self, who wanted to discover what would happen to the ship in the future and how to prevent it. Frantic, the future Picard tried to depart in the
           <i>
            El-Baz
           </i>
           again, but his past counterpart decided that it was time "to end the cycle" and killed him with a phaser. The
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           was then able to escape the vortex. (
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Time_Squared_(episode)" title="Time Squared (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Time Squared (TNG 2x13)">
             Time Squared
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </li>
          <li>
           In
           <a href="/wiki/2366" title="2366">
            2366
           </a>
           , the
           <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-C)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-C)">
            USS
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
            -C
           </a>
           emerged from a
           <a href="/wiki/Temporal_rift" title="Temporal rift">
            temporal rift
           </a>
           . Its disappearance from the year
           <a href="/wiki/2344" title="2344">
            2344
           </a>
           caused an
           <a href="/wiki/Alternate_timeline" title="Alternate timeline">
            altered timeline
           </a>
           , where the Federation was losing
           <a href="/wiki/Federation-Klingon_War_(alternate_timeline)" title="Federation-Klingon War (alternate timeline)">
            a war
           </a>
           against the
           <a href="/wiki/Klingon_Empire" title="Klingon Empire">
            Klingon Empire
           </a>
           . Picard was still the USS
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -D's commanding officer, though more toughened due to the horrors of war. Upon Guinan's advice, Picard decided to send the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -C back to the past. After Captain
           <a href="/wiki/Rachel_Garrett" title="Rachel Garrett">
            Rachel Garrett
           </a>
           was killed during a
           <a href="/wiki/Klingon" title="Klingon">
            Klingon
           </a>
           attack, Picard allowed
           <a href="/wiki/Richard_Castillo" title="Richard Castillo">
            Richard Castillo
           </a>
           to assume command and return the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           -C to
           <a href="/wiki/2344" title="2344">
            2344
           </a>
           . (
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Yesterday%27s_Enterprise_(episode)" title="Yesterday's Enterprise (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Yesterday's Enterprise (TNG 3x15)">
             Yesterday's Enterprise
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </li>
         </ul>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           "Yesterday's Enterprise" Director
           <a href="/wiki/David_Carson" title="David Carson">
            David Carson
           </a>
           noted, "
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Patrick_Stewart" title="Patrick Stewart">
           Patrick Stewart
          </a>
          loved playing that war-like captain in a war situation after 20 years of war.
          <i>
           "
          </i>
          <span class="noicon">
           <a class="external autonumber exitstitial" href="http://www.startrek.com/article/david-carson-revisits-his-trek-days-part-1" rel="nofollow">
            [1]
           </a>
          </span>
          <i>
          </i>
         </div>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/13/Picard%2C_lieutenant_junior_grade.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140805224238&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Picard, lieutenant junior grade" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Picard%2C_lieutenant_junior_grade.jpg" data-image-name="Picard, lieutenant junior grade.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/13/Picard%2C_lieutenant_junior_grade.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140805224238&amp;path-prefix=en" height="145" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard, lieutenant junior grade" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard%2C_lieutenant_junior_grade.jpg" data-image-name="Picard, lieutenant junior grade.jpg" height="145" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/1/13/Picard%2C_lieutenant_junior_grade.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140805224238&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard,_lieutenant_junior_grade.jpg">

            Lieutenant junior grade Jean-Luc Picard
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <ul>
          <li>
           In an alternate timeline created by Q, Picard was given the chance to walk away from his fight with the
           <a href="/wiki/Nausicaan" title="Nausicaan">
            Nausicaan
           </a>
           that caused serious injury to his heart, forcing a
           <a href="/wiki/Artificial_heart" title="Artificial heart">
            bionic replacement
           </a>
           to be installed. When he returned to the present, Picard was a mere lieutenant junior grade, with Worf as his supervisor. This was because his near-death experience made the young Picard realize just how fragile life was and how important it could be, thus making him even more determined to make his mark in the universe and take risks; as it was, all Picard learned from the incident was to play it safe and not take risks. Picard convinced Q to allow him to correct the damage to his timeline and returned to his reality (although it was never confirmed whether this
           <i>
            actually
           </i>
           happened or if it was just a near-death hallucination). (
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Tapestry_(episode)" title="Tapestry (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Tapestry (TNG 6x15)">
             Tapestry
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </li>
          <li>
           In
           <a href="/wiki/2370" title="2370">
            2370
           </a>
           , Lieutenant Worf encountered a
           <a href="/wiki/Quantum_fissure" title="Quantum fissure">
            quantum fissure
           </a>
           which caused him to begin shifting between
           <a href="/wiki/Quantum_reality" title="Quantum reality">
            quantum realities
           </a>
           . In several universes, Picard was still captain of the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           and attended a surprise birthday party for Worf, though his services were stated to be required on the bridge. In the final universe in which Worf arrived, William Riker was the captain, as Picard was lost in the Borg encounter of
           <a href="/wiki/2367" title="2367">
            2367
           </a>
           . In another reality, the Borg had invaded the Federation and the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           was one of the few ships left. Worf was finally returned to his own quantum reality and the quantum fissure was sealed. (
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Parallels_(episode)" title="Parallels (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Parallels (TNG 7x11)">
             Parallels
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </li>
         </ul>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/a/a1/Picard2395.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120921115619&amp;path-prefix=en">

           <noscript>
            <img alt="Picard2395" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Picard2395.jpg" data-image-name="Picard2395.jpg" height="195" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/a/a1/Picard2395.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120921115619&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Picard2395.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">

           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <ul>
          <li>
           In
           <a href="/wiki/2370" title="2370">
            2370
           </a>
           , while standing trial by Q, Picard's consciousness was shifting between three alternate timelines. In
           <a href="/wiki/Anti-time_past" title="Anti-time past">
            an alternate 2364
           </a>
           , Picard disobeyed Starfleet orders from the moment he arrived on board the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           at Earth Station McKinley. He called a red alert while docked at the station, ordered the ship to the Devron system instead of to Farpoint Station and took the vessel into a temporal anomaly there. In
           <a href="/wiki/Anti-time_present" title="Anti-time present">
            an alternate 2370
           </a>
           , Picard was diagnosed with
           <a href="/wiki/Irumodic_Syndrome" title="Irumodic Syndrome">
            Irumodic Syndrome
           </a>
           by Dr. Crusher. This caused her to reconsider her relationship with Picard, and she reversed her earlier decision to remain just friends. The
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           was dispatched to the Devron system near the Romulan Neutral Zone where it discovered the temporal anomaly. In an
           <a href="/wiki/Anti-time_future" title="Anti-time future">
            unknown, alternate future timeframe
           </a>
           , Picard found himself at his family's vineyard with Geordi La Forge. Picard contacted Riker, now an
           <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">
            admiral
           </a>
           and
           <a href="/wiki/Commanding_officer" title="Commanding officer">
            commanding officer
           </a>
           of
           <a href="/wiki/Starbase_247" title="Starbase 247">
            Starbase 247
           </a>
           , for help in investigating the anomaly, but Riker refused to allow him passage to the Neutral Zone, thinking Picard had been affected by his Irumodic Syndrome and was delusional. Later, Picard convinced his ex-wife, Beverly Picard, to take her medical ship, the
           <a href="/wiki/USS_Pasteur" title="USS Pasteur">
            USS
            <i>
             Pasteur
            </i>
           </a>
           , to investigate the anomaly. The
           <i>
            Pasteur
           </i>
           was attacked and destroyed by
           <a href="/wiki/Negh%27Var_warship" title="Negh'Var warship">
            Klingon battleships
           </a>
           , but the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           , under command of Admiral Riker, arrived to rescue the crew and fight off the Klingons. Picard once again pleaded with Riker to return to the
           <a href="/wiki/Devron_system" title="Devron system">
            Devron system
           </a>
           , but he was then sedated and returned to quarters. Armed with new information gathered from the other two timeframes, Picard woke and went to talk to Riker and the other former
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           officers, and convinced them that the anomaly existed. The
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           returned just in time to watch it form, and Riker ordered the
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           into the anomaly, where it used a
           <a href="/wiki/Static_warp_shell" title="Static warp shell">
            static warp shell
           </a>
           in concert with the other
           <i>
            Enterprise
           </i>
           s to collapse it. After the anomaly was sealed, the timelines were erased, and only Picard retained memory of those events. He told his staff of his experiences in the future, in hopes that things such as the conflict between Worf and Riker that followed Deanna Troi's death never happen. (
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/All_Good_Things..._(episode)" title="All Good Things... (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="All Good Things... (TNG 7x25/26)">
             All Good Things...
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </li>
          <li>
           Picard was briefly trapped in the
           <a href="/wiki/Nexus" title="Nexus">
            Nexus
           </a>
           during a mission to stop renegade
           <a href="/wiki/El-Aurian" title="El-Aurian">
            El-Aurian
           </a>
           <a href="/wiki/Scientist" title="Scientist">
            scientist
           </a>
           Dr.
           <a href="/wiki/Tolian_Soran" title="Tolian Soran">
            Tolian Soran
           </a>
           from destroying the
           <a href="/wiki/Veridian_system" title="Veridian system">
            Veridian system
           </a>
           . In the perfect world in the Nexus, his nephew Ren (who had recently died in a fire) was still alive, and he had a wife and four children. Realizing that it wasn't real, he rejected the reality offered to him and left the Nexus to defeat Soran with the aid of Captain
           <a href="/wiki/James_T._Kirk" title="James T. Kirk">
            James T. Kirk
           </a>
           . (
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Generations" title="Star Trek Generations">
             <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek Generations">
              Star Trek Generations
             </span>
            </a>
           </i>
           )
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Holograms">
           Holograms
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit Holograms section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px">
          <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/0/08/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2383.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140304183736&amp;path-prefix=en">
           <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, 2383" class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2383.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, 2383.jpg" data-src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/0/08/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2383.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140304183736&amp;path-prefix=en" height="181" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="180"/>
           <noscript>
            <img alt="Jean-Luc Picard, 2383" class="thumbimage " data-image-key="Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2383.jpg" data-image-name="Jean-Luc Picard, 2383.jpg" height="181" src="http://vignette3.wikia.nocookie.net/memoryalpha/images/0/08/Jean-Luc_Picard%2C_2383.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140304183736&amp;path-prefix=en" width="180"/>
           </noscript>
          </a>
          <figcaption>
           <a class="sprite info-icon" href="/wiki/File:Jean-Luc_Picard,_2383.jpg">
           </a>
           <p class="caption">
            Picard as an Admiral in Barash's holoprogram
           </p>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <ul>
          <li>
           As part of
           <a href="/wiki/Reginald_Barclay" title="Reginald Barclay">
            Reginald Barclay
           </a>
           's
           <a href="/wiki/Holo-addiction" title="Holo-addiction">
            holo-addiction
           </a>
           , he had created at least two programs that had recreations of Jean-Luc. One was a recreation of the
           <a href="/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(NCC-1701-D)" title="USS Enterprise (NCC-1701-D)">
            USS
            <i>
             Enterprise
            </i>
            -D
           </a>
           , the other,
           <a href="/wiki/Barclay_Program_15" title="Barclay Program 15">
            Barclay Program 15
           </a>
           , had Picard as one of
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/The_Three_Musketeers" title="The Three Musketeers">
             The Three Musketeers
            </a>
           </i>
           . (
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Hollow_Pursuits_(episode)" title="Hollow Pursuits (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Hollow Pursuits (TNG 3x21)">
             Hollow Pursuits
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </li>
          <li>
           A Jean-Luc Picard
           <a href="/wiki/Holographic_duplicate#Picard.2C_Jean-Luc" title="Holographic duplicate">
            hologram
           </a>
           was in
           <a href="/wiki/Barash" title="Barash">
            Barash
           </a>
           's
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Holoprogram" title="Holoprogram">
            holoprogram
           </a>
           , this future Picard was a full
           <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">
            admiral
           </a>
           . (
           <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             TNG
            </span>
           </a>
           : "
           <a href="/wiki/Future_Imperfect_(episode)" title="Future Imperfect (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="Future Imperfect (TNG 4x08)">
             Future Imperfect
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </li>
         </ul>

         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Catchphrases">
           Catchphrases
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit Catchphrases section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          "
          <i>
           Make it so!
          </i>
          "
         </p>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           - His order for implementing an idea just suggested (
           <i>
            <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_The_Next_Generation" title="Star Trek: The Next Generation">
             Star Trek: The Next Generation
            </a>
           </i>
           )
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <div style="border:1px dotted #666666; padding:0.5em; font-family:cambria,serif; margin: 1em 1em 1em 3em;">
          <i>
           According to
           <a href="/wiki/Robert_Justman" title="Robert Justman">
            Robert Justman
           </a>
           , this was a homage to Captain
           <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horatio_Hornblower" title="wikipedia:Horatio Hornblower">
            Horatio Hornblower
           </a>
           , who gave the same command in novels by
           <a class="extiw exitstitial" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C.S._Forrester" title="wikipedia:C.S. Forrester">
            C.S. Forrester
           </a>
           . (
          </i>
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek_Encyclopedia" title="Star Trek Encyclopedia">
           Star Trek Encyclopedia
          </a>
          <i>
           2nd ed., p. 172)
          </i>
         </div>
         <p>
          "
          <i>
           Engage.
          </i>
          "
         </p>
         <dl>
          <dd>
           - Another famous order typically in reference to going into warp (

           </i>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="References_by_other_people">
           References by other people
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit References by other people section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2369" title="2369">
           2369
          </a>
          , after Vash arrived on Deep Space 9,
          <a href="/wiki/Miles_O%27Brien" title="Miles O'Brien">
           Miles O'Brien
          </a>
          told
          <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Sisko" title="Benjamin Sisko">
           Benjamin Sisko
          </a>
          about her relationship with Picard. While Sisko replied "
          <i>
           Somehow she doesn't seem to be his type,
          </i>
          " O'Brien thought it was because Picard "likes a good challenge." Later, when Q placed Sisko in a
          <a href="/wiki/Boxing" title="Boxing">
           boxing
          </a>
          match, he was shocked after Sisko knocked him to the ground. "
          <i>
           You hit me... Picard never hit me!
          </i>
          ", to which Sisko shot back, "
          <i>
           I'm
          </i>
          not
          <i>
           Picard!
          </i>
          " (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
            DS9
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Q-Less_(episode)" title="Q-Less (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Q-Less (DS9 1x07)">
            Q-Less
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2372" title="2372">
           2372
          </a>
          , Worf and Miles O'Brien reminisced in
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quark%27s" title="Quark's">
           Quark's
          </a>
          about rescuing Picard from the Borg Collective. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
            DS9
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/The_Way_of_the_Warrior_(episode)" title="The Way of the Warrior (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Way of the Warrior (DS9 4x01/02)">
            The Way of the Warrior
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Later that year, after a
          <a href="/wiki/Quinn" title="Quinn">
           member of the Q Continuum
          </a>
          arrived on her ship seeking asylum,
          <a href="/wiki/Kathryn_Janeway" title="Kathryn Janeway">
           Kathryn Janeway
          </a>
          automatically assumed he was Picard's
          <a href="/wiki/Q" title="Q">
           Q
          </a>
          - which instead made him nervous and agitated. When that Q, tasked with capturing the renegade, appeared on the bridge, she realized that
          <i>
           he
          </i>
          was the being she'd heard so much about, he laughed and asked her, "
          <i>
           Has Jean-Luc been whispering about me behind my back?
          </i>
          " (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Voyager" title="Star Trek: Voyager">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Voyager">
            VOY
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Death_Wish_(episode)" title="Death Wish (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Death Wish (VOY 2x18)">
            Death Wish
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In her effort to look through every log entry of Starfleet captains who had contact with the Borg, Captain Janeway cited Picard's words among others: "
          <i>
           In their collective state, the Borg are utterly without mercy  driven by one will alone, the will to conquer. They are beyond redemption, beyond reason
          </i>
          ", with
          <a href="/wiki/Chakotay" title="Chakotay">
           Chakotay
          </a>
          claiming that she had unknowingly mimicked Picard's vocal mannerisms while quoting him. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Voyager" title="Star Trek: Voyager">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Voyager">
            VOY
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Scorpion_(episode)" title="Scorpion (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Scorpion (VOY 3x26)">
            Scorpion
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/2375" title="2375">
           2375
          </a>
          , Ensign
          <a href="/wiki/Nog" title="Nog">
           Nog
          </a>
          mentioned
          <a href="/wiki/Al_Lorenzo" title="Al Lorenzo">
           Al Lorenzo
          </a>
          having a curious interest in taking holophotos of himself sitting behind the desks of famous Starfleet captains. Usually, he would sneak into their offices, but the
          <a href="/wiki/Dominion_War" title="Dominion War">
           Dominion War
          </a>
          made it difficult for him to get away. Among the photos in his collection included Lorenzo sitting behind the desks of such famous commanders as
          <a href="/wiki/Robert_DeSoto" title="Robert DeSoto">
           Robert DeSoto
          </a>
          and Jean-Luc Picard. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Deep_Space_Nine" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Deep Space Nine">
            DS9
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Treachery,_Faith_and_the_Great_River_(episode)" title="Treachery, Faith and the Great River (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Treachery, Faith and the Great River (DS9 7x06)">
            Treachery, Faith and the Great River
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <p>
          Q mentioned "Jean-Luc" as another option for helping to raise his son to the satisfaction of the Q Continuum. He wondered aloud if it was not too late to ask Picard instead of Janeway. (
          <a href="/wiki/Star_Trek:_Voyager" title="Star Trek: Voyager">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Star Trek: Voyager">
            VOY
           </span>
          </a>
          : "
          <a href="/wiki/Q2_(episode)" title="Q2 (episode)">
           <span style="cursor: help;" title="Q2 (VOY 7x19)">
            Q2
           </span>
          </a>
          ")
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Quotes_about_Picard">
           Quotes about Picard
          </span>
          <span class="editsection">
           <a href="/wiki/Jean-Luc_Picard?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit Quotes about Picard section">
            <img class="sprite edit-pencil" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D"/>
            Edit
           </a>
          </span>
         </h3>

          <i>
           ...the heart of an explorer, and the soul of a poet.
          </i>
          "

             Skin of Evil
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </dd>
         </dl>
         <p>

          <i>
           I've never known anyone with more drive, determination or more courage than Jean-Luc Picard.
          </i>
          "
          <br/>
         </p>

          <dd>
           -
           <b>
            Admiral J.P Hanson
           </b>
           , ("
           <a href="/wiki/The_Best_of_Both_Worlds,_Part_II_(episode)" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (episode)">
            <span style="cursor: help;" title="The Best of Both Worlds, Part II (TNG 4x01)">
             The Best of Both Worlds, Part II
            </span>
           </a>
           ")
          </dd>
         </dl>

          <i>
           Jean-Luc, I never knew you were such a
          </i>
          cad
          <i>
           . I'm impressed.

         </p>

          <dd>

           <b>

           </b>

            </span>

          </dd>
